# Architecture Guide: Project Knot

This document explains the purpose of each file and folder for future developers.

---

## Project Structure Overview

```
Knot/
├── memory-bank/               # Documentation and planning
│   ├── PRD.md                 # Product Requirements Document
│   ├── techstack.md           # Technology stack decisions
│   ├── IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md # Step-by-step build instructions
│   ├── progress.md            # Implementation progress log
│   └── architecture.md        # This file
├── iOS/                       # iOS application (Swift/SwiftUI)
└── backend/                   # Python/FastAPI backend
```

---

## iOS Application (`iOS/`)

### Configuration Files

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `project.yml` | XcodeGen configuration. Defines targets, build settings, and dependencies. Run `xcodegen generate` after modifying. **Step 19.0:** the `Knot` target carries a `postBuildScript` ("Inject Dev API Host") that runs `scripts/inject-dev-host.sh` to write the Mac's LAN IP into a bundled `DevServer.plist` for DEBUG on-device/simulator testing. Because `ENABLE_USER_SCRIPT_SANDBOXING` is on, the phase declares the script path under `inputFiles` (so the sandbox may read it) and `DevServer.plist` under `outputFiles` (a separate file from `Info.plist` to avoid a "multiple commands produce" conflict). |
| `scripts/inject-dev-host.sh` | **Step 19.0.** DEBUG-only postBuild script: detects the Mac's private LAN IP (`en0`…`en8`, first 192.168/10/172.16-31 address) and writes `DevAPIBaseURL = http://<ip>:8000` into `Knot.app/DevServer.plist`; falls back to `127.0.0.1` when offline. Read by `Constants.API.resolveDebugBaseURL`. Detection logic mirrors `backend/scripts/dev.sh`. |
| `Knot.xcodeproj/` | Generated Xcode project. **Do not edit directly** — modify `project.yml` instead. |
| `Knot/Info.plist` | iOS app configuration (bundle name, supported orientations, launch screen). |
| `Knot/Knot.entitlements` | App entitlements file. Contains `com.apple.developer.applesignin` for Sign in with Apple and `aps-environment: development` for push notifications (Step 7.4). Referenced by `CODE_SIGN_ENTITLEMENTS` in `project.yml`. Both the entitlements plist and `project.yml` must stay in sync for XcodeGen. |

### Source Code (`iOS/Knot/`)

#### `/App` — Application Entry Point
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `KnotApp.swift` | Main app entry point. Configures SwiftData ModelContainer and injects it into the app environment. **Step 7.4:** Added `@UIApplicationDelegateAdaptor(AppDelegate.self) var appDelegate` to bridge UIKit delegate callbacks into the SwiftUI lifecycle. **Step 9.1:** Added `@State private var deepLinkHandler = DeepLinkHandler()`, injects it via `.environment(deepLinkHandler)` on ContentView. **Step 15.2:** Updated `.onOpenURL` to route auth callback URLs (`com.ronniejay.knot://login-callback`) to `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session(from:)` for OAuth/magic link session exchange; other URLs still forwarded to `deepLinkHandler.handleURL(url)`. |
| `ContentView.swift` | Root auth state router. Creates `AuthViewModel` as `@State`, injects it into the SwiftUI environment via `.environment()`, and starts the `authStateChanges` listener via `.task`. Routes between three states: loading spinner (`isCheckingSession`), `MainTabView` (`isAuthenticated` + `hasCompletedOnboarding`), or `SignInView` (default). **Step 9.1:** Added `@Environment(DeepLinkHandler.self) private var deepLinkHandler` for deep link navigation readiness (consumed in Step 9.2). **Step 16.1:** Replaced `HomeView()` with `MainTabView()` for authenticated+onboarded state. Deep link `fullScreenCover` remains on ContentView, overlaying the entire tab bar. |
| `MainTabView.swift` | **Active (Step 16.1, redesigned in Step 18.3, slimmed in Step 18.6).** Root 3-tab container that replaces SwiftUI's `TabView` with a `ZStack` content router plus a custom `KnotTabBar` mounted via `.safeAreaInset(edge: .bottom)`. Tabs: For You (`sparkles` → `ForYouView()`), Saved (`bookmark`/`bookmark.fill` → `SavedView()`), Profile (`person.crop.circle`/`person.crop.circle.fill` → `SettingsView(isTabEmbedded: true)`) — all SF Symbols. All three destinations are mounted simultaneously and toggled via `.opacity` + `.allowsHitTesting` + `.accessibilityHidden` so view-tree identity (and view-model lifetimes) survive tab switches the same way `TabView` preserves them. Hoists `NetworkMonitor` as `@State` and injects via `.environment(networkMonitor)` so all tabs can access connectivity state. Defines `AppTab` enum (Int raw values: forYou=0, saved=1, profile=2). **Step 18.6:** Removed the standalone `Hints` tab (`HintsTabView`); hint capture now lives inside the recommendation refresh flow via `SessionHintsSheet` so the captured signal immediately influences the next set of recommendations rather than disappearing into a separate surface. The previous `UITabBarAppearance` plumbing, `findTabBars(in:)` window-traversal hack, `@Environment(\.colorScheme)` observer, and `import LucideIcons` were all deleted in Step 18.3 — the SwiftUI primitive owns all visuals, so trait-collection-aware `Theme` tokens propagate automatically. |
| `AppDelegate.swift` | **Active (Step 7.4).** `@MainActor final class` conforming to `UIApplicationDelegate` and `@preconcurrency UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate`. Handles APNs remote notification registration callbacks that SwiftUI cannot access natively. `didFinishLaunchingWithOptions` sets `UNUserNotificationCenter.current().delegate = self` for foreground notification display. `didRegisterForRemoteNotificationsWithDeviceToken` converts raw `Data` to hex string and calls `DeviceTokenService.shared.registerToken()`. `didFailToRegisterForRemoteNotificationsWithError` logs gracefully (expected on Simulator). `userNotificationCenter(_:willPresent:)` returns `[.banner, .sound]` for foreground notification display. Uses `@preconcurrency` on `UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate` to resolve Swift 6 strict concurrency errors with non-Sendable `UNUserNotificationCenter`/`UNNotification` parameters. |

#### `/Features` — Feature Modules
Organized by feature, each containing Views, ViewModels, and feature-specific components.

| Folder | Status | Purpose |
|--------|--------|---------|
| `Auth/` | **Active** | Multi-provider sign-in (Apple, Google, Email magic link), session management, auth state |
| `Home/` | **Active (Step 16.1)** | Home tab — header, hint capture, milestone countdown, recent hints, offline banner. Recommendations button, saved section, and settings gear removed (moved to Discover, Saved, Profile tabs). |
| `Onboarding/` | **Active** | Partner Vault creation (9-step wizard). Container + ViewModel at root, step views in `Steps/` subfolder. |
| `ForYou/` | **Active (Step 16.2)** | For You tab — milestone timeline with integrated recommendation CTAs and "just because" card. |
| `Recommendations/` | **Active (Step 16.2)** | Choice-of-Three UI, recommendation cards, refresh flow. Now pushed from ForYouView with optional milestone context. |
| `HintCapture/` | Planned | Text and voice hint input |
| `Notifications/` | **Active (Step 7.7)** | Notification History screen showing past milestone notifications with recommendation detail. |
| `Saved/` | **Active (Step 16.1)** | Saved tab — full list of bookmarked recommendations from SwiftData (no limit). |
| `Settings/` | **Active (Step 17.1)** | Settings screen (account, partner profile, milestones, notifications with quiet hours, privacy, about), Edit Profile screen, account deletion flow with re-authentication, and notification preferences management. Embedded in Profile tab via `isTabEmbedded` parameter. **Step 17.1:** Added "Milestones" navigation row opening `MilestonesManagementView` via `.fullScreenCover`. |
| `Milestones/` | **Active (Step 17.1)** | Post-onboarding milestone management UI. Add/edit/delete milestones from Settings. |

##### `Auth/` — Authentication Feature
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `SignInView.swift` | Sign-in screen with two-section layout: 55% photo grid (top) + 45% dark-gradient branding section (bottom). **PhotoGridSection** (private struct): 4 rows of photo tiles from 20 images in `Assets.xcassets/SignIn/` namespace (signin-0 through signin-19, 5 unique per row). Continuous horizontal scrolling animation via `TimelineView` — even rows (0, 2) scroll right, odd rows (1, 3) scroll left. Each row has 10 tiles (2 copies of 5-image pattern) for seamless infinite looping. Offset computed from continuous time with modulo (`cycleDuration: 12` seconds). **BrandingSection** (private struct): Lucide heart icon, two-tone "Knot" title, "Connect Deeply" tagline pinned near top (24pt top padding), `Spacer()` between tagline and CTA, single "Get Started" button navigates to `LoginView` via `NavigationLink(value: "getStarted")`. Navigation destination routes `"getStarted"` → `LoginView()` and `"magicLink"` → `MagicLinkView()`. Loading overlay with `ProgressView` during sign-in. **Step 15.4:** Removed "I already have an account" button; restructured BrandingSection to pin branding at top with button at bottom. **Step 18.20:** Three performance fixes to `PhotoGridSection` to stop continuous main-thread saturation that was making the entire app feel sluggish on real devices. (1) Added `@State isVisible` + `.onAppear` / `.onDisappear` so the `TimelineView` subtree is removed when the view goes off-screen — handles SwiftUI view-tree retention after auth/navigation. The off-state renders a static first-frame snapshot via the new `gridContent(at:singleSetWidth:tileWidth:tileHeight:)` `@ViewBuilder` helper so layout doesn't jump if visibility flips. (2) Swapped `TimelineView(.animation)` (display-refresh rate: 60-120 Hz) for `TimelineView(.periodic(from: .now, by: 1.0 / 30.0))` (capped at 30 fps) — 2-4× reduction in per-second work, visually indistinguishable on the 12-second scroll cycle. (3) Added `.drawingGroup()` to the tile `VStack` so SwiftUI composes the 40-tile grid off-screen via Metal, moving the per-frame composite from the main thread to the GPU. Combined, these reduce the section's main-thread cost from "one core pegged" to negligible. |
| `LoginView.swift` | **Active (Step 15.4).** Multi-provider login screen reached via "Get Started" from SignInView. "Create Account" title in accent color with subtitle "Sign up to start building your partner vault". Three white pill-shaped buttons (54pt height, `RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: 27)`, black text on white): (1) **Continue with Apple** — plain `Button` calling `authViewModel.signInWithApple()` with Apple logo SF Symbol; (2) **Continue with Google** — calls `authViewModel.signInWithGoogle()` with custom `GoogleLogoIcon` (gradient "G" text); (3) **Continue with Email** — `NavigationLink(value: "magicLink")` with Lucide `mail` icon. Loading overlay during auth. Dark background (`Theme.backgroundGradient`). |
| `MagicLinkView.swift` | **Active (Step 15.4).** Two-state email magic link view. **Email input state:** Lucide `mail` icon, "Enter your email" title, subtitle "We'll send you a magic link to create your account.", email `TextField` (`.emailAddress` keyboard, surface background, accent border on focus), "Send Magic Link" button (disabled when empty, coral-pink when active). **Confirmation state:** Lucide `mailCheck` icon, "Check your email" title, recipient email in bold, "Resend Email" text button. State toggle via `@State private var isSent: Bool`. Only transitions to sent state if no error occurred. **Step 18.19:** Added `.contentShape(Rectangle()) + .onTapGesture { isEmailFocused = true }` on the field's outer card so taps anywhere on the rounded envelope focus the field. Replaced the immediate `.onAppear { isEmailFocused = true }` auto-focus with `.task { try? await Task.sleep(for: .milliseconds(300)); isEmailFocused = true }` to defer focus past the screen's present animation — on real devices the immediate-onAppear focus request races with the responder chain and the keyboard never opens automatically. |
| `AuthViewModel.swift` | `@Observable @MainActor` class managing the full auth lifecycle. On launch, listens to `authStateChanges` to restore sessions from Keychain (`initialSession` event). **Apple Sign-In:** `signInWithApple()` uses programmatic `ASAuthorizationController` (not `SignInWithAppleButton`) with OIDC nonce security. Bridges delegate callbacks to async/await via `AppleSignInDelegate` (private `NSObject` class using `CheckedContinuation`). Replaced the previous invisible `SignInWithAppleButton` overlay pattern which failed to receive touches. **Step 15.2:** Added `sendMagicLink(email:)` — calls `SupabaseManager.client.auth.signInWithOTP(email:redirectTo:shouldCreateUser:)` to send passwordless magic link email. **Step 15.3:** `signInWithGoogle()` uses native Google Sign-In SDK (`GIDSignIn.sharedInstance.signIn(withPresenting:)`) to get Google ID token, then forwards to Supabase via `signInWithIdToken(provider: .google, idToken:)`. Handles user cancellation (`GIDSignInError.canceled`) silently. Requires "Skip nonce checks" enabled for Google in Supabase dashboard. Both methods use existing `isLoading`/`signInError`/`showError` pattern. Provides `signOut()` (Step 2.4), `signOutAfterDeletion()` (Step 11.2). All auth state transitions flow through `listenForAuthChanges()`. **Step 7.4:** `requestPushNotificationPermission()` called after vault check. |

##### `Home/` — Home Feature
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `HomeView.swift` | **Active (Step 11.1, slimmed in Step 18.6).** Home screen with 3 sections: (1) **Offline banner** — red `HStack` with Lucide `wifiOff` icon, animated show/hide via `.transition(.move(edge: .top).combined(with: .opacity))`, driven by `networkMonitor.isConnected`; (2) **Header** — time-of-day greeting (`greetingText` switches on `Calendar.current.component(.hour)`), partner name (32pt bold, `minimumScaleFactor(0.7)` for long names), next milestone countdown badge (circular 64×64, `milestoneCountdownColor()` returns red/orange/yellow/pink by urgency), milestone subtitle with SF Symbol icon, and horizontally scrollable vibe capsule tags (`vibeDisplayName()` converts snake_case → Title Case inline); (3) **Upcoming Milestones** — `ForEach(viewModel.upcomingMilestones)` renders `milestoneCard()` with SF Symbol type icon, name, `formattedDate`, countdown capsule pill, urgency coloring; loading spinner and dashed-border `emptyMilestoneCard`. The **Hint Capture** input and **Recent Hints** preview that previously lived here were removed in Step 18.6 alongside the standalone Hints tab — hint capture is now contextual to the recommendation refresh flow via `SessionHintsSheet`, which makes the captured signal feel useful (it shapes the next set of cards) rather than dropping into a write-only history surface. Saved Recommendations preview also no longer lives here (moved to the dedicated Saved tab in Step 16.1). All interactive sections `.disabled(!networkMonitor.isConnected).opacity(0.5)` when offline. Toolbar: Knot branding (heart + "Knot") leading. `.task { await viewModel.loadVault() }` on appear. `.scrollDismissesKeyboard(.interactively)`. **Step 9.2:** Added `@Environment(DeepLinkHandler.self) private var deepLinkHandler` and `@State private var deepLinkRecommendationId: String?` for deep-link navigation via `.fullScreenCover(isPresented:)`. |
| `HomeViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 18.6, slimmed).** `@Observable @MainActor` class managing Home screen vault data only. **Vault data:** `loadVault()` calls `VaultService().getVault()` and stores the `VaultGetResponse` in `vault`. Computed properties: `partnerName` (fallback "Your Partner"), `upcomingMilestones` (parses all milestones via `parseMilestoneDate()`, computes `daysUntilNextOccurrence()` with year rollover, sorts by proximity, returns top 2 as `[UpcomingMilestone]`), `nextMilestone` (first upcoming), `vibes` (vault's vibe tags). **Helpers:** `parseMilestoneDate(_:)` splits "2000-MM-DD" into (month, day) tuple; `daysUntilNextOccurrence(month:day:from:calendar:)` tries current year first, falls back to next year if date passed. Also defines `UpcomingMilestone` (Identifiable, Sendable — id, name, type, month, day, daysUntil, budgetTier; computed `formattedDate`, `countdownText` with Today!/Tomorrow/in X days, `iconName` SF Symbol per milestone type, `urgencyLevel` enum critical/soon/upcoming/distant). **Step 18.6:** Removed hint submission/loading (`submitHint`, `loadRecentHints`, `recentHints`, `isSubmittingHint`, `showHintSuccess`, `hintErrorMessage`), the `HintPreview` struct, and the `parseISO8601` helper (sole caller was `loadRecentHints`). Saved-recommendations logic had already been moved out of HomeViewModel to `SavedViewModel` in Step 16.1. |

##### `Settings/` — Settings & Profile Editing
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `SettingsView.swift` | **Active (Step 11.4).** Settings screen presented as a `.sheet` from HomeView's gear toolbar button. Five grouped sections: (1) **Account** — email info row (loaded from `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session.user.email`), Sign Out action (delegates to `authViewModel.signOut()`), Delete Account with three-stage deletion flow (Step 11.2); (2) **Partner Profile** — Edit Profile row opens `EditVaultView` via `.fullScreenCover`; (3) **Notifications** — Enable Notifications toggle (reads `UNUserNotificationCenter` status, toggles via permission request or system Settings redirect), **Quiet Hours (Step 11.4)** — expandable section with start/end hour pickers (0-23, formatted as 12-hour time via `viewModel.formatHour()`), tapping the row toggles `showQuietHoursPicker`, `Picker` wheels for start and end hours, loading/saving indicators, preferences loaded from backend via `NotificationPreferencesService` on `.task`; (4) **Privacy** — Export My Data with confirmation alert + working export pipeline (Step 11.3), Clear All Hints with destructive confirmation alert and sequential `HintService.deleteHint()` calls; (5) **About** — Version info row (`Bundle.main` version + build), Terms of Service and Privacy Policy (open external URLs). Three reusable private row builders: `settingsRow` (tappable with icon/title/subtitle/chevron, mirrors `EditVaultView.editSectionButton` pattern), `settingsInfoRow` (non-tappable with right-aligned value), `settingsToggleRow` (with `Toggle` control). `sectionHeader` renders uppercase caption labels. Dismiss via X button in toolbar. **Step 11.2 account deletion:** Three-stage flow: Stage 1 (warning `.alert`) → Stage 2 (`ReauthenticationSheet` via `.sheet`) → Stage 3 (final confirmation `.alert` → `executeAccountDeletion()` → `signOutAfterDeletion()` → dismiss). Deletion loading overlay (`ProgressView` + "Deleting account..." over semi-transparent background) shown when `isDeletingAccount`. Error alert for `deleteAccountError`. **Step 11.3 data export:** Confirmation alert → `exportUserData()` → export loading overlay ("Exporting your data..." ProgressView) → share sheet via `UIActivityViewController` wrapped in private `ShareSheet: UIViewControllerRepresentable`. Export error alert for `exportDataError`. Share sheet presented via `.sheet(isPresented: $viewModel.showExportShareSheet)` with the temp file URL. **Architecture note:** 8+ chained `.alert` modifiers caused Swift type checker timeout; resolved by extracting alerts into two `ViewModifier` structs: `AccountDeletionAlerts` (warning, final confirmation, error alerts) and `SettingsAlerts` (clear hints, hints cleared, export confirmation, export error, general error alerts). Toolbar extracted into `settingsToolbar` computed property. `@Environment(\.modelContext)` injected for SwiftData local data cleanup during deletion. **Step 18.1:** Migrated to `Components/UI/` primitives — every section uses `KnotSectionHeader(.caption)` instead of the private `sectionHeader` helper; every row uses `KnotListRow.chevron`/`info`/`toggle`/`action` static factories instead of the private `settingsRow`/`settingsInfoRow`/`settingsToggleRow` helpers (all three were deleted). The Quiet Hours expandable row uses the generic `KnotListRow` initializer with a custom trailing chevron that swaps between up/down with the expanded state. Toolbar X button became `KnotIconButton(.ghost, .sm)`. Both deletion and export loading overlays became `KnotProgressIndicator.Overlay(message:)`. The expanded quiet-hours panel is wrapped in a `KnotCard(padding: .none, radius: Theme.Radius.md)`. |
| `SettingsViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 11.4).** `@Observable @MainActor` state management for `SettingsView`. **State:** `userEmail` (loaded async from Supabase session), `notificationsEnabled` (reads `UNUserNotificationCenter` authorization status), `isClearingHints`/`clearHintsError`/`showClearHintsSuccess` (hint clearing flow), `showDeleteAccountAlert`/`showExportDataAlert` (alert triggers), `isUpdatingNotifications` (toggle loading). **Step 11.2 deletion state:** `showReauthentication: Bool` (controls re-auth sheet), `showFinalDeleteConfirmation: Bool` (controls final alert), `isDeletingAccount: Bool` (loading overlay), `deleteAccountError: String?` (error display), `isReauthenticated: Bool` (tracks re-auth success). **Step 11.3 export state:** `isExportingData: Bool` (loading overlay), `exportDataError: String?` (error alert), `showExportShareSheet: Bool` (triggers share sheet), `exportedFileURL: URL?` (temp file for sharing). **Step 11.4 notification preferences state:** `quietHoursStart: Int` (0-23, default 22), `quietHoursEnd: Int` (0-23, default 8), `isLoadingPreferences: Bool`, `isSavingPreferences: Bool`, `preferencesError: String?`, `showQuietHoursPicker: Bool`. **Computed:** `appVersion` reads `CFBundleShortVersionString` and `CFBundleVersion` from `Bundle.main.infoDictionary`. **Actions:** `loadUserEmail()` gets email from `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session.user.email`; `loadNotificationStatus()` checks `UNUserNotificationCenter.current().notificationSettings()` for `.authorized` status; `toggleNotifications()` handles iOS permission lifecycle — requests permission when disabled, opens system Settings when enabled (iOS cannot revoke programmatically); `clearAllHints()` paginates through all hints via `HintService.listHints(limit: 100, offset: 0)` in a while loop. **Step 11.2 deletion methods:** `requestAccountDeletion()` → shows warning alert; `confirmDeleteAndReauthenticate()` → shows re-auth sheet; `onReauthenticationSuccess()` → sets `isReauthenticated`, hides re-auth, shows final confirmation; `onReauthenticationFailure()` → resets re-auth state; `executeAccountDeletion(modelContext:) async → Bool` → calls `AccountService().deleteAccount()`, then `clearLocalData(modelContext:)`. **Step 11.3 export method:** `exportUserData() async` → calls `ExportService().exportData()`, renders styled PDF via `PDFExportRenderer().renderPDF(from:)`, writes to temp file, triggers share sheet. **Step 11.4 notification preferences methods:** `loadNotificationPreferences() async` → calls `NotificationPreferencesService().fetchPreferences()`, populates `quietHoursStart`/`quietHoursEnd` from response; `saveQuietHours() async` → calls `NotificationPreferencesService().updatePreferences()` with current start/end values, updates state from response; `formatHour(_ hour: Int) -> String` → converts 0-23 integer to 12-hour format string (e.g., 22 → "10:00 PM", 0 → "12:00 AM"). Uses `import SwiftData` and `import Foundation`. |
| `ReauthenticationSheet.swift` | **Active (Step 15.5).** Filename kept for Xcode project-file compatibility but the contents are now a **typed-confirmation sheet** that works for all auth providers (Apple, Google, Email). The user must type `DELETE ACCOUNT` (case-sensitive, exact match) to enable the destructive submit button. On submit it calls the parent-provided `onConfirm: () async -> Bool` closure, which runs `SettingsViewModel.executeAccountDeletion(modelContext:)` and signs the user out on success. Layout: `Lucide.shieldAlert` icon (red, 48pt), "Delete Account" title, body text about the 60-day grace + restore option, `TextField` bound to a local `@State var typedConfirmation: String`, destructive `Button` (full width, 54pt) — disabled until `typedConfirmation == "DELETE ACCOUNT"`. Cancel (X) button in toolbar calls `onCancel` + dismisses. `interactiveDismissDisabled(isSubmitting)` prevents accidental dismissal mid-request. `NavigationStack` with "Delete Account" inline title, `Theme.backgroundGradient` background. |
| `PendingDeletionView.swift` | **Active (Step 15.5).** Full-screen gate presented by `ContentView` when the signed-in user's account is in the 60-day deletion grace window (`AuthViewModel.pendingDeletionScheduledAt != nil`). Layout: red `Lucide.shieldAlert` icon (56pt), "Account Pending Deletion" title, body text with the formatted scheduled deletion date, two buttons — "Restore Account" (calls `AccountService().restoreAccount()` then invokes `onRestored`) and "Sign Out" (calls the `onSignOut` async closure). On successful restore, `AuthViewModel.didRestoreAccount()` clears the pending flag and re-runs the vault check so the user lands directly on Home or Onboarding without resigning in. Public API: `init(scheduledAt: Date, onRestored: () -> Void, onSignOut: () async -> Void)`. |
| `EditVaultView.swift` | **Active (Step 3.12, updated Step 18.13).** Full-screen Edit Profile screen accessible from SettingsView. On appear, calls `VaultService.getVault()` to load existing vault data from `GET /api/v1/vault`, then creates a fresh `OnboardingViewModel` and populates all its properties (basic info, interests, dislikes, milestones, vibes, budgets, love languages) from the response. **Step 18.32:** `loadVaultData()` also sets `hasSetBirthday` / `hasSetAnniversary` true when seeding an existing birthday/anniversary so the edit flow shows the saved date (not the placeholder) and the new required-selection validation never blocks an edit. Displays a sectioned list of 7 `editSectionButton` cards (icon + title + subtitle + chevron), each opening the corresponding edit sheet via `.sheet(item: $activeSection)`. Uses local `EditSection` enum (Identifiable, 7 cases — independent of `OnboardingStep`). Sheet content for basic-info/milestones/budget/love-languages routes to the composite `Edit*Sheet` views under `EditSheets/`; interests/dislikes/vibes still use the corresponding single-question onboarding step views directly since they were already single-screen. "Save" toolbar button calls `vm.buildVaultPayload()` and `VaultService.updateVault(_:)` (`PUT /api/v1/vault`). Subtitle helper for love languages uses `LoveLanguageDisplay.name(for:)` from the Shared/ helpers. |

**`EditSheets/` — Single-page composites that mirror the pre-split onboarding (Step 18.13)**

These reuse the original full-screen layouts so a user editing their profile from Settings sees all of a section's inputs at once instead of paging through a 4-screen flow. Each sheet binds to the same `OnboardingViewModel` data the onboarding flow writes, so saving via `VaultService.updateVault()` works without translation.

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `EditBasicInfoSheet.swift` | Composite for editing partner name + tenure + cohabitation + location in a single ScrollView. Pre-split this was `OnboardingBasicInfoView`. Validation reads `viewModel.canProceed` against the `.partnerName` and `.location` rules. **Step 18.29:** the inline dual `Picker(.menu)` `tenureSection` (and its private `tenureSummary`) were replaced by the shared `RelationshipLengthField` (labeled "How long have you been together?"), so tenure editing here uses the same stepper dialog as onboarding. |
| `EditMilestonesSheet.swift` | Composite for editing birthday + anniversary + holidays + custom milestones in a single ScrollView. Pre-split this was `OnboardingMilestonesView`. Uses its own file-private `HolidayChip` and `monthPicker`/`dayPicker` helpers (which don't collide with the shared `milestoneMonthPicker` family — different names). |
| `EditBudgetSheet.swift` | Composite for editing all three budget tiers in a single ScrollView. Since **Step 18.35** renders three `BudgetTierSliderCard`s (shared) bound directly to `viewModel.justBecauseMin/Max` / `.minorOccasionMin/Max` / `.majorMilestoneMin/Max` via `@Bindable`. Visually identical to the consolidated onboarding budget step — everything routes through `Steps/Shared/BudgetTierSliderCard.swift` + `BudgetRangeSlider.swift`. |
| `EditLoveLanguagesSheet.swift` | Composite for editing primary + secondary love languages from one card grid. Uses the shared `LoveLanguageCard` and `LoveLanguageSelectionState` types, plus its own `selectLanguage(_:)` method that implements the 5-branch toggle (tap primary clears both, tap secondary clears secondary, no primary sets primary, no secondary sets secondary, both set replaces secondary). The onboarding `OnboardingLoveLanguagesView` (re-merged in **Step 18.38**) collects the same two picks but with a "promote secondary up" rule on primary deselect rather than clearing both. |

##### `ForYou/` — Milestone Timeline + Recommendations (Step 16.2)
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `ForYouView.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1).** Main For You tab view. NavigationStack with "For You" title and "+" toolbar button for adding milestones. ScrollView containing JustBecauseCard at top, "Upcoming" section header, chronological milestone timeline (ForEach over MilestoneItemResponse), and empty state. NavigationLinks push RecommendationsView with milestone context. Pull-to-refresh reloads milestones. Sheet presents MilestoneFormSheet (reused from Milestones/). **Step 18.1:** Migrated the "Upcoming" section header to `KnotSectionHeader` and the empty-state "Add Your First Milestone" CTA to `KnotButton(.primary, .sm, .pill)`. **Step 18.18:** Removed the full-screen `ProgressView` branch that previously hid the entire screen during initial milestone load. `timelineContent` now renders unconditionally so the `JustBecauseCard` is tappable from the first frame; the loading state moved inline into the timeline section as a centered spinner with vertical padding, leaving the "Surprise them today" entry point always available. |
| `ForYouViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 16.2).** `@Observable @MainActor` view model managing timeline data. Loads milestones via MilestoneService.listMilestones() and partner name via VaultService.getVault() in parallel. Provides urgencyLevel(for:) with 5-tier MilestoneUrgency enum, formattedDate(_:) for "MMM d" display, and occasionType(for:) mapping. Does not own recommendation state — each NavigationLink push creates a fresh RecommendationsView. |
| `TimelineEntryView.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1).** Individual milestone row in the vertical timeline. Leading: timeline line (2px) + urgency-colored dot (10px). Content: date badge (capsule), milestone icon + name, countdown text. Optional "Get Recommendations" CTA card (shown when daysUntil <= 60) with accent-colored background and chevron. **Step 18.1:** Date pill migrated to `KnotBadge(.secondary, .sm)`; the tinted-soft "Get Recommendations" CTA was deliberately kept inline as a snowflake design (doesn't justify a new primitive variant). |
| `JustBecauseCard.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1).** Top card for non-milestone recommendation generation. Sparkles icon, "Surprise them today" title, description with partner name, pink "Get Recommendations" CTA button. **Step 18.1:** Migrated to compose `KnotCard` + `KnotSectionHeader` + `KnotButton` primitives instead of inline chrome. `onGenerate` is typed `@MainActor () -> Void` for Swift 6 strict concurrency. |

##### `Milestones/` — Post-Onboarding Milestone Management (Step 17.1)
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `MilestonesManagementView.swift` | **Active (Step 17.1).** Full-screen milestone management UI presented from Settings. Grouped list by milestone type with type-colored icons, days-until badges, swipe-to-delete, context menu (edit/delete). Contains `MilestoneFormSheet` for add/edit with month/day pickers, type picker, recurrence toggle, budget tier picker. "Add Milestone" button in toolbar. Empty state with guidance text. Uses `MilestonesViewModel` for state management. |
| `MilestonesViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 17.1).** `@Observable @MainActor` state management for milestone CRUD. Properties: `milestones: [MilestoneItemResponse]`, form fields (`formName`, `formType`, `formMonth`, `formDay`, `formRecurrence`, `formBudgetTier`). Methods: `loadMilestones()`, `prepareAdd()`, `prepareEdit(_:)`, `saveMilestone()` (creates or updates based on editing state), `deleteMilestone()`. Uses `MilestoneService` for API calls. |

##### `Recommendations/` — Spotlight Deck + Detail Page (Step 18.43)
**Step 18.43 superseded the discovery presentation.** Earlier iterations: a Choice-of-Three horizontal pager (Steps 6.2–18.4) → a Rappi/DoorDash-style vertical scroll feed of `RecommendationCard`s (Step 18.5). Step 18.43 replaced the feed with a **Spotlight** experience inspired by Blinkist (one-at-a-time 👍/👎 voting via `SpotlightDeckView` + `SpotlightCard`) and Airbnb (an immersive `RecommendationDetailView` for every type). The detail page is shared by the main For You loop (`RecommendationsView`) and the onboarding reveal (`OnboardingCompletionView`); both still drive the unchanged `RecommendationsViewModel`. **Step 18.45** redesigned `SpotlightCard` into a full-bleed immersive card (cream chips + title + description + a pink "See Details" button overlaid on the photo) and split the two surfaces' containers: For You keeps the swipe/vote `SpotlightDeckView`, while the onboarding reveal switched to the new **browse-only `SpotlightCarouselView`** (paged `TabView` + page dots, no save/pass voting). `RecommendationCard.swift` is retained for reference but is no longer the primary surface. The structured idea-section renderers were extracted into the shared `IdeaContentSectionsView`, and `MatchingFactorChip` + the chip builder into `RecommendationChips`. **Step 18.49** unified the two surfaces: the main For You loop (`RecommendationsView`) switched from the swipe/vote `SpotlightDeckView` to the same browse-only `SpotlightCarouselView` as the onboarding reveal, so the post-onboarding "get recommendations" experience is now identical to the in-onboarding one (no save/pass voting, no Refresh / Adjust Vibe — saving happens on the detail page). `SpotlightDeckView` is no longer wired into any live surface but is retained (and still unit-tested) for reference.
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `SpotlightDeckView.swift` | **Active (Step 18.43; card redesigned Step 18.45). Primary For You discovery surface.** A Blinkist-style swipe/vote deck rendering one `SpotlightCard` at a time from `viewModel.recommendations`. Owns only a `@State index` and the drag/fling animation; persistence, feedback, detail presentation, and top-up are delegated to the host via closures (`isSaved`, `onLike`, `onPass`, `onOpenDetail`, `onNeedMore`) plus `isLoadingMore` and `resetToken`. **Interactions:** below the card, two circular buttons — 👎 pass (`Lucide.thumbsDown`, calls `onPass` → records `disliked`) and 👍 save (`Lucide.thumbsUp`, calls `onLike` → saves) — plus a `DragGesture` (drag past `swipeThreshold = 110` → like right / pass left) with rotation + "SAVE"/"PASS" stamps. The card opens detail via its own in-card "See Details" button (`onSeeDetails` → `onOpenDetail`); the Step 18.43 whole-card `.onTapGesture` was removed in 18.45. A slim dot/progress row (`{i} of {n}`) sits on top. `advance()` increments the index and fires `onNeedMore` when past the last card; `onChange(of: resetToken)` snaps back to index 0 (fresh generate / full refresh) without disturbing an append top-up. End-of-deck state: a spinner while `isLoadingMore`, else a "That's all for now" card. **`SpotlightCard`** (same file, **redesigned Step 18.45**): a full-bleed image card (`ZStack(alignment: .bottom)`, 22pt rounded clip, `maxHeight: .infinity`) — image fills the whole card via `Color.clear.overlay { image.scaledToFill() }.clipped()`, with a light top scrim (type badge + saved indicator legibility) and a heavy bottom scrim. Overlaid at the bottom: cream `MatchingFactorChip(onImage: true)` chips in a `FlowLayout`, a white Fraunces title (2-line), a white `item.description` (≤4 lines, newly surfaced), and a full-width pink "See Details" `KnotButton` (`onSeeDetails`). The old image-hero + white `detailsSection`, the `merchant · price · location` meta line (`MetaPart`/`metaParts`/`locationText`), the "Tap for details" affordance, and the personalization snippet were removed. **`SpotlightCarouselView`** (same file, **new Step 18.45**): the browse-only counterpart used by the onboarding reveal — a paged `TabView` of `SpotlightCard`s (`.tabViewStyle(.page(indexDisplayMode: .never))`) with custom page dots (shown only when `items.count > 1`), parameters `items` / `partnerName` / `isSaved` / `onOpenDetail`. No voting, no top-up. 2 `#Preview`s (deck + carousel). |
| `RecommendationDetailView.swift` | **Active (Step 18.43, Airbnb-style detail page).** One immersive full-screen detail surface for **every** recommendation type, opened by tapping a deck card. Replaces `SelectionConfirmationSheet` as the destination and is a strict superset of `IdeaDetailView`. **Layout:** a 320pt collapsing hero (`AsyncImage` + type-specific fallback gradient + scrims, type badge) with overlaid circular back/share/save buttons; title + meta (`merchant · price · location`); a **"Why Knot picked this for {partner}"** card elevating `personalization_note` with the matched vibes/love-languages/interests as proof badges; an "About" description; a "Where" location row (experiences/dates); and the structured idea content via the shared `IdeaContentSectionsView` (Knot Originals). A `safeAreaInset(.bottom)` **sticky bar** pins price + the primary CTA — "Open in {Merchant}" for purchasables (→ `onOpenMerchant`, the existing handoff) or "Save to Library" for ideas (→ `onSave`). Save state is optimistic/local (`@State savedLocally`, synced from `isSaved` on appear, one-way flip) so the heart + CTA update on tap without coupling to the VM. Params: `item`, `partnerName: String?` (falls back to "your partner"), `isSaved`, and `onOpenMerchant`/`onSave`/`onShare`/`onDismiss` closures. 2 `#Preview`s (gift, idea) + a shared `PreviewRecommendations` JSON-decode helper used by both new view files. |
| `IdeaContentSectionsView.swift` | **Active (Step 18.43, extracted from `IdeaDetailView`).** Renders the `[IdeaContentSection]` of a Knot Original by `type`: `overview` (accent left-border paragraph), `steps` (numbered cards), `setup`/`variations` (icon lists), `tips` (yellow box), `conversation` (chat bubbles), `budget_tips` (green box), `music`/`food_pairing` (icon cards), with a generic fallback. Hosted by both `IdeaDetailView` (which now delegates to it) and `RecommendationDetailView`. Configurable inter-section `spacing` (default 24). |
| `RecommendationChips.swift` | **Active (Step 18.43, shared; `onImage` variant added Step 18.45).** `MatchingFactorChip` (promoted from `private` in `RecommendationCard`) — a color-coded match badge (interest = accent/heart, vibe = purple/sparkles, love language = orange/hand). An `onImage: Bool = false` flag (Step 18.45) switches it to a uniform cream "on-image" pill (fixed cream fill `#FFF0E0`, dark text, 13pt, no icon, no border) for legibility overlaid on a photo — used by the immersive `SpotlightCard`; the default colored/icon appearance is unchanged for the detail page and legacy feed card. `RecommendationDisplayChip` + its `build(vibes:loveLanguages:interests:)` builder produce the ordered display chips (vibes → love languages → interests, keys resolved via `OnboardingVibesView.displayName` / `LoveLanguageDisplay.name`). Used by `RecommendationCard`, `SpotlightCard`, and `RecommendationDetailView`. |
| `RecommendationCard.swift` | **Active (Step 18.5, redesigned for vertical feed; Step 18.43 retained for reference, no longer the primary surface — chip code moved to `RecommendationChips.swift`, `orderedChips` now uses `RecommendationDisplayChip.build`).** Standalone SwiftUI view displaying a single recommendation card in the vertical scroll feed. Layout: (1) **Hero section** (220pt tall — Step 18.5 grew from 160pt; vertical scroll affords taller cards with no viewport-fit constraint) — `AsyncImage` with 3-phase handling (loading: gradient + spinner, success: resizable fill image clipped to `heroHeight`, failure: type-specific gradient fallback with a large semi-transparent SF Symbol centered). Type-specific fallback gradients: pink/purple for gifts, blue/indigo for experiences, orange/pink for dates, yellow/orange for ideas. Two gradient overlays: a top-edge gradient (`.black.opacity(0.35) → .clear`) for top-overlay legibility, and a bottom-edge gradient (Step 18.5) for the personalization overlay's legibility. (2) **Hero overlay row** — top-left type badge (`Capsule` with `.ultraThinMaterial` fill, Lucide icon + uppercase label "GIFT"/"EXPERIENCE"/"DATE"/"IDEA"/"DATE PLAN"); top-right price chip (frosted-capsule, white text, shows `~$49` for `priceConfidence == "estimated"`, hidden when `priceCents` is nil); top-right circular icon-only Save button (Lucide `bookmark` ↔ `bookmarkCheck`, accent-tinted when `isSaved`, frosted-circle background). (3) **Hero bottom-left overlay** (Step 18.5) — `personalizationOverlay(note:)` renders a frosted `RoundedRectangle` with `✨ <note>` (Lucide `sparkles` + italic) when `personalizationNote` is non-empty, mirroring Rappi's "ordered recently" badge pattern. When `personalizationNote` is nil/empty, the overlay is omitted and the description renders in the body section instead — the card never shows both. (4) **Details section** (16pt padding) — Title (`.headline.weight(.semibold)`, 2-line limit, `fixedSize` vertical); restaurant-style **meta line** (Step 18.5) — `🏪 Merchant · 💰 $49 · 📍 City, State` rendered as a horizontal row of `MetaPart` items separated by inline dot dividers, with each part conditionally rendered when its data is present (`merchantName`, formatted `priceCents`, `[locationCity, locationState].joined`); description fallback (when `personalizationNote` was empty); matched chips rendered unbounded in a `FlowLayout` (Step 18.5 removed the Step 18.4 cap-of-3 + `+N` overflow). Chips are ordered vibes → love languages → interests (most personality-rooted first), wrapping to multiple rows naturally. (5) **Full-width Select / Read button** — `KnotButton(.primary, .md, .pill)` with trailing icon (Lucide `arrowRight` for regular recs, `book` for ideas/plans). **Parameters:** `title`, `descriptionText`, `recommendationType`, `priceCents`, `currency`, `priceConfidence`, `merchantName: String?` (Step 18.5 restored from Step 18.4 removal), `imageURL`, `isSaved: Bool`, `matchedInterests`/`matchedVibes`/`matchedLoveLanguages`, `personalizationNote: String?`, `locationCity: String?` and `locationState: String?` (Step 18.5 new), `onSelect`/`onSave` closures. **Helpers:** `formattedPrice(cents:currency:)` (unchanged) — locale-aware currency formatter, `internal` for test access, omits decimals for whole-dollar amounts. **File-private types:** `MetaPart` struct (Step 18.5) holds `icon + text` for the restaurant-style meta line; `DisplayChip` struct (carried over from Step 18.4) holds `label + style` for priority ordering. The Step 18.4 `.overflow` `MatchingFactorChip.ChipStyle` case was deleted in Step 18.5 since unbounded chips don't need an overflow indicator. **Concurrency:** All closures typed as `@MainActor @Sendable () -> Void`. Card corner radius: 18pt. 4+ `#Preview` variants exercising hero with personalization overlay, no-personalization with description fallback, missing merchant/location, and many-chips wrapping. |
| `RecommendationsView.swift` | **Active (Step 18.5, vertical feed).** Full-screen SwiftUI view for the recommendations surface. Presented as a `NavigationStack` with back button (Lucide `arrowLeft`) and "Recommendations" title. Four states: (1) **Loading** — `ForYouLoadingView` with 5 orbiting Lucide icons and cycling messages (Step 14.9). (2) **Error** — `alertCircle` icon, error message, and "Try Again" button that re-triggers generation. (3) **Empty** — `sparkles` icon with prompt to complete partner vault. (4) **Content** — Step 18.5 **vertical scroll feed**: a `ScrollView` containing a `LazyVStack(spacing: 16)` that renders all `RecommendationCard` components stacked vertically (Rappi/DoorDash-style menu rather than the previous Choice-of-Three horizontal pager). The page indicator and the `TabView(.page)` pager from Steps 6.2–18.4 were removed — vertical scroll has natural progress affordance. The `pageIndicator` private computed property is now vestigial dead code (kept intentionally to keep the v2 → main diff focused on the layout swap; safe to remove in a follow-up cleanup). **Action buttons** ("Adjust Vibe" + "Refresh") render below the scroll feed via the Step 18.3 sibling-VStack pattern with `.padding(.bottom, 100)` — `safeAreaInset` from `MainTabView` does not propagate through `navigationDestination` pushes, so explicit clearance for `KnotTabBar` is required. The buttons render only when `showActionButtons` is true (mirrors `recommendationsContent`'s state guards: `!isLoading && !isPlayingClimax && errorMessage == nil && !recommendations.isEmpty`). Refresh button calls `viewModel.requestRefresh()` (shows reason sheet); disabled during `isRefreshing` or `!cardsVisible`. The previous `.opacity(cardsVisible ? 1 : 0)` and `.scaleEffect(cardsVisible ? 1 : 0.85)` exit/entry animations from Step 6.4 were preserved on the scroll feed. **Step 6.3:** Added `.sheet(isPresented: $viewModel.showConfirmationSheet)` presenting `SelectionConfirmationSheet` with `.presentationDetents([.medium])`. Wired `onSelect` callback on each `RecommendationCard` to `viewModel.selectRecommendation(item)`. Contains `SelectionConfirmationSheet` struct — bottom sheet with type badge (SF Symbol + label), title, description, merchant + price row, location row, "Open in [Merchant]" confirm button, and "Cancel" button. Uses Lucide icons `store`, `mapPin`, `externalLink`. Helpers: `formattedPrice(cents:currency:)`, `typeIconSystemName`, `typeLabel`, `confirmButtonLabel`. **Step 6.4:** Added card exit/entry animations — `TabView` and page indicator use `.opacity(cardsVisible ? 1 : 0)` and `.scaleEffect(cardsVisible ? 1 : 0.85)` with `.animation(.easeInOut(duration: 0.3))`. Added refresh loading overlay — centered `ProgressView` with "Finding better options..." text shown in a `ZStack` over the `TabView` when `isRefreshing` is true, with `.transition(.opacity)`. Refresh button now calls `viewModel.requestRefresh()` (shows reason sheet) instead of direct refresh; disabled during `isRefreshing` or `!cardsVisible`. Added second `.sheet(isPresented: $viewModel.showRefreshReasonSheet)` presenting `RefreshReasonSheet` with `.presentationDetents([.medium])`. Contains `RefreshReasonSheet` struct — bottom sheet with "Why are you refreshing?" header and 5 rejection reason buttons: "Too expensive" (`arrow.up.circle`), "Too cheap" (`arrow.down.circle`), "Not their style" (`hand.thumbsdown`), "Already have something similar" (`doc.on.doc`), "Just show me different options" (`arrow.triangle.2.circlepath`). Each button is a full-width row with SF Symbol icon, label, and chevron in a `Theme.surface` rounded rectangle. Uses `.buttonStyle(.plain)`. **Step 6.6:** Wires `isSaved`, `onSave` callbacks into each `RecommendationCard` in the `TabView` (the `onShare` callback was removed in Step 18.4 — `viewModel.shareRecommendation` is still used by the saved view and confirm sheet). Injects `@Environment(\.modelContext)` and passes it to ViewModel via `viewModel.configure(modelContext:)` in `.task`. **Step 9.4:** Added `@Environment(\.scenePhase) private var scenePhase` and `.onChange(of: scenePhase)` that calls `viewModel.handleReturnFromMerchant()` on `background → active` transition. Added `.sheet(isPresented: $viewModel.showPurchasePromptSheet)` presenting `PurchasePromptSheet` with `.presentationDetents([.medium])` — wires `onConfirmPurchase` to `viewModel.confirmPurchase()`, `onSaveForLater` to `viewModel.declinePurchaseAndSave()`, `onDismiss` to `viewModel.dismissPurchasePrompt()`. Added `.sheet(isPresented: $viewModel.showRatingPrompt)` presenting `PurchaseRatingSheet` with `.presentationDetents([.medium])` — wires `onSubmit` to `viewModel.submitPurchaseRating(_:feedbackText:)`, `onSkip` to `viewModel.skipPurchaseRating()`. **Step 10.4:** Added `import StoreKit` and `@Environment(\.requestReview) private var requestReview`. Added `.sheet(isPresented: $viewModel.showAppReviewPrompt)` presenting `AppReviewPromptSheet` with `.presentationDetents([.medium])` — `onAccept` records prompt date via `viewModel.recordAppReviewPromptDate()`, dismisses sheet, waits 500ms, then calls `requestReview()` from the environment; `onDecline` calls `viewModel.dismissAppReviewPrompt()`. The `requestReview()` call must originate from a SwiftUI View (not the ViewModel) because it's an `@Environment` value. Four `#Preview` blocks: Loading, Gift confirmation, Experience with location, Refresh Reason Sheet. **Step 14.9 animation structs (file-private, defined after `RecommendationsView`):** `ForYouLoadingView` — full-screen loading animation with 5 Lucide icons (gift, heart, star, shoppingBag, sparkles) orbiting a central pulsing sparkles icon via `TimelineView(.animation)` (60fps, no manual timer); 4 contextual messages cycle every 2.5s with a fade via `Timer.publish` + `.onReceive`. `RefreshLoadingOverlay` — compact floating card with a pulsing sparkles icon shown over existing cards during a refresh, replacing the old bare spinner. **Step 17.1:** Added `briefingCard()` view builder — conversational briefing card displayed above page indicator when `viewModel.briefingText` is non-nil. Shows Lucide `messageCircle` icon, accent-tinted background, briefing text in conversational style. Updated `onSelect` handler to open idea detail view for both `"idea"` and `"plan"` recommendation types. **Step 18.42:** `ForYouLoadingView` and `ForYouClimaxView` were changed from `private struct` to internal `struct` so the onboarding recommendation-reveal step (`OnboardingCompletionView`) can reuse the exact same loading + celebration animations. No behavior change here. **Step 18.49:** the content state now renders the browse-only `SpotlightCarouselView` (the onboarding reveal's container) instead of `SpotlightDeckView`, making the main-app reveal identical to onboarding. Removed the bottom action bar ("Adjust Vibe" + "Refresh") and its `showActionButtons`/`adjustVibeButton`/`refreshButton` helpers, the `RefreshLoadingOverlay` struct, and the refresh-reason / session-hint / vibe-override `.sheet` presentations (now unreachable). The carousel carries `.padding(.bottom, 100)` for `KnotTabBar` clearance. The `RefreshReasonSheet`/`SessionHintsSheet`/`VibeOverrideSheet` struct definitions and the related `RecommendationsViewModel` refresh/vote methods remain as dead code pending a later cleanup. The error-state "Try Again" button and all purchase-handoff sheets are unchanged. |
| `RecommendationsViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 17.1).** `@MainActor @Observable` state container for the recommendations screen. **Step 17.1:** Added `briefingText: String?` property populated from `response.briefingText` in `generateRecommendations()`. Properties: `recommendations: [RecommendationItemResponse]` (current set of up to 3), `isLoading` (initial generation), `isRefreshing` (refresh in progress), `errorMessage`, `currentPage` (TabView selection), `hasLoadedInitially: Bool` (prevents re-fetching recommendations on tab switch; set `true` after first successful `generateRecommendations()` call; the `.task` modifier in `RecommendationsView` guards on this flag so returning to the tab doesn't trigger a new API call). **Step 6.3 selection state:** `selectedRecommendation: RecommendationItemResponse?`, `showConfirmationSheet: Bool`. **Step 6.4 refresh reason state:** `showRefreshReasonSheet: Bool`, `cardsVisible: Bool` (defaults `true`, controls card opacity/scale for enter/exit animations). **Step 6.6 save/share state:** `savedRecommendationIds: Set<String>` (in-memory dedup set hydrated from SwiftData), `modelContext: ModelContext?` (injected via `configure(modelContext:)`). **Step 9.4 return-to-app state:** `pendingHandoffRecommendation: RecommendationItemResponse?` (set in `confirmSelection()`, cleared when purchase prompt is resolved), `showPurchasePromptSheet: Bool` (triggers purchase prompt sheet), `showRatingPrompt: Bool` (triggers rating sheet after "Yes"). **Step 10.4 app review state:** `showAppReviewPrompt: Bool` (triggers App Store review prompt sheet after 5-star rating). Methods: `generateRecommendations(occasionType:milestoneId:)` calls `RecommendationService.generateRecommendations()` and populates the array; `refreshRecommendations(reason:)` collects current recommendation IDs, calls `RecommendationService.refreshRecommendations()`, and replaces the array. Both methods guard against duplicate calls, reset `currentPage` to 0, and clear `errorMessage` before starting. **Step 6.3 methods:** `selectRecommendation(_:)` stores item and shows sheet; `confirmSelection()` records "selected" feedback (fire-and-forget), opens merchant URL via `MerchantHandoffService` (Step 9.3), dismisses confirmation sheet, preserves `pendingHandoffRecommendation` for return-to-app prompt (Step 9.4); `dismissSelection()` clears state. **Step 6.4 methods:** `requestRefresh()` shows the refresh reason sheet, guarded against duplicate calls when `isRefreshing` or `!cardsVisible`; `handleRefreshReason(_ reason:)` orchestrates the full refresh flow — dismiss sheet → medium haptic → 300ms pause → set `cardsVisible = false` (exit animation) → 350ms pause → call `refreshRecommendations(reason:)` → set `cardsVisible = true` (entry animation) → success haptic. Uses `Task.sleep` for timing coordination between SwiftUI animations and state changes. **Step 6.6 methods:** `configure(modelContext:)` sets the context and calls `loadSavedIds()`; `isSaved(_:)` checks `savedRecommendationIds` set; `saveRecommendation(_:)` creates `SavedRecommendation` SwiftData object, inserts via modelContext, updates dedup set, records "saved" feedback to backend; `shareRecommendation(_:)` presents `UIActivityViewController` via root view controller with formatted message (title + merchant + price + URL), records "shared" feedback; `loadSavedIds()` fetches all `SavedRecommendation` objects and populates the dedup set. **Step 9.4 methods:** `handleReturnFromMerchant()` guards pending handoff, 500ms delay via `Task.sleep`, shows purchase prompt; `confirmPurchase()` records "purchased" feedback, dismisses prompt, shows rating prompt with success haptic; `submitPurchaseRating(_:feedbackText:)` records "rated" feedback with rating/text, clears all state, then if rating == 5 and 90-day cooldown elapsed: 2-second delay + shows app review prompt (Step 10.4); `skipPurchaseRating()` clears state without recording; `declinePurchaseAndSave()` reuses `saveRecommendation()` then clears state; `dismissPurchasePrompt()` clears all return-to-app state. **Step 10.4 methods:** `canPromptForAppReview()` checks UserDefaults `lastAppReviewPromptDate` and returns true if 90+ days elapsed or never prompted; `recordAppReviewPromptDate()` stores current date; `dismissAppReviewPrompt()` clears `showAppReviewPrompt` flag. Rate-limit constants: `appReviewPromptKey` (UserDefaults key), `reviewCooldownDays = 90`. Dependency-injected `RecommendationService` via init parameter for testability. **Step 15.2 background loading state:** `backgroundTaskID: UIBackgroundTaskIdentifier` (`.invalid` when no background task is active), `wasBackgroundedWhileLoading: Bool` (set `true` when the app backgrounds while `isLoading` or `isRefreshing`). **Step 15.2 methods:** `handleAppBackgroundedWhileLoading()` guards on `isLoading \|\| isRefreshing`, calls `UIApplication.shared.beginBackgroundTask` (with `@MainActor`-dispatched expiration handler), sets `wasBackgroundedWhileLoading = true`, schedules "Still working on it…" local notification (1s delay, identifier `"knot.recs.loading"`). `cancelPendingLoadingNotification()` resets `wasBackgroundedWhileLoading`, removes pending notifications for both `"knot.recs.loading"` and `"knot.recs.ready"`. `completeBackgroundLoadingIfNeeded()` (private) checks `wasBackgroundedWhileLoading` flag and `backgroundTaskID`, schedules "Your picks are ready ✨" notification (0.5s trigger, identifier `"knot.recs.ready"`, `.default` sound), then ends the background task. Called at the end of both `generateRecommendations()` and `refreshRecommendations()` before clearing their loading flags. `endBackgroundExecution()` (private) calls `UIApplication.shared.endBackgroundTask()` and resets identifier to `.invalid`. `scheduleStillLoadingNotification()` and `scheduleReadyNotification()` (both private) create `UNMutableNotificationContent` + `UNTimeIntervalNotificationTrigger` and add via `UNUserNotificationCenter`. Ready notification uses 0.5s trigger (not `nil`) because `nil` triggers fail to deliver from background. **Step 18.43 Spotlight deck state:** `partnerName: String?` (best-effort `VaultService().getVault()` load kicked off from `configure`, for the detail header), `isLoadingMore: Bool` (drives the deck's "Finding more…" end state), `selectedDetailItem: RecommendationItemResponse?` (drives the detail `fullScreenCover(item:)`), `deckResetToken: Int` (bumped on a wholesale replace in `generateRecommendations`/`refreshRecommendations` so the deck resets to card 0; **not** bumped by an append top-up). **Step 18.43 methods:** `recordDislike(_:)` (light haptic + fire-and-forget `"disliked"` feedback — the deck advances locally regardless), `loadMoreForDeck()` (guards on empty/in-flight, appends a deduped fresh batch via `service.refreshRecommendations(reason: "show_different")` with the seen IDs excluded — no replace/animation, sets `isLoadingMore`), `openDetail`/`dismissDetail`, and `openMerchantFromDetail(_:)` (mirrors `confirmSelection` but takes the item directly and dismisses the detail first, since the detail page is itself the confirmation surface — records `"selected"`, preserves `pendingHandoffRecommendation`, opens the merchant URL). |

| `PurchasePromptSheet.swift` | **Active (Step 9.4).** Bottom sheet presented when the user returns to Knot after a merchant handoff. Asks "Did you complete your purchase?" with shopping bag icon (Lucide `shoppingBag`), item title, and optional merchant name. Two action buttons: "Yes, I bought it!" (accent-filled `RoundedRectangle`, Lucide `check` icon) triggers `onConfirmPurchase`, "No, save for later" (surface-filled with border, Lucide `bookmark` icon) triggers `onSaveForLater`. Accepts primitive fields (`title: String`, `merchantName: String?`) rather than typed recommendation items so it works with both `RecommendationItemResponse` (main flow) and `MilestoneRecommendationItemResponse` (deep link flow). All closures typed as `@MainActor @Sendable () -> Void` for Swift 6 strict concurrency. Presented with `.presentationDetents([.medium])` and `.presentationDragIndicator(.visible)`. `onDismiss` closure for drag-to-dismiss cleanup. 2 preview variants (with merchant, without merchant). |
| `PurchaseRatingSheet.swift` | **Active (Step 9.4).** Bottom sheet for optional post-purchase feedback. Header: "How was this pick?" with sparkles icon (Lucide `sparkles`) and item title. 5-star rating selector using SF Symbols (`star.fill` for selected, `star` for unselected) in gold (`Color.yellow`), with light haptic feedback (`UIImpactFeedbackGenerator(.light)`) on each tap. Optional `TextEditor` for free-text notes (3–6 line axis, placeholder overlay "Any notes? (optional)"). "Submit" button (accent-filled, disabled when `rating == 0`) and "Skip" text button below. All state managed locally via `@State` (`rating: Int`, `feedbackText: String`). Closures: `onSubmit: (Int, String?) -> Void` and `onSkip: () -> Void`. Presented with `.presentationDetents([.medium])`. 1 preview variant. |
| `AppReviewPromptSheet.swift` | **Active (Step 10.4).** Bottom sheet asking the user if they'd like to share their experience via App Store review. Shown after a 5-star purchase rating with a 2-second delay, rate-limited to once per 90 days. Header: Lucide `heart` icon (36pt, accent-colored) + "Glad you loved it!" title (`.title3.weight(.bold)`) + "Would you like to share your experience with others?" body text (`.subheadline`, `Theme.textSecondary`, center-aligned). Divider separates header from action buttons. "Yes, let's do it!" accept button (accent-filled `RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: 14)`, Lucide `star` icon + semibold label). "Not now" decline button (surface-filled with `surfaceBorder` stroke). Callbacks: `onAccept: @MainActor @Sendable () -> Void`, `onDecline: @MainActor @Sendable () -> Void`. Follows the exact visual pattern of `PurchasePromptSheet` and `PurchaseRatingSheet`. Presented with `.presentationDetents([.medium])` and `.presentationDragIndicator(.visible)`. The accept callback in `RecommendationsView` records the prompt date, dismisses the sheet, waits 500ms, then calls `requestReview()` from `@Environment(\.requestReview)`. 1 preview variant. |
| `DeepLinkRecommendationView.swift` | **Active (Step 9.4).** Full-screen view for displaying a single recommendation opened via Universal Link deep link. Presented as `fullScreenCover` from `HomeView` when `deepLinkRecommendationId` is set. Takes `recommendationId: String` and `onDismiss` closure. Fetches the recommendation via `RecommendationService.fetchRecommendation(id:)` (`GET /api/v1/recommendations/{id}`) in `.task`. Three states: (1) **Loading** — centered `ProgressView` with "Loading recommendation..." text. (2) **Error** — `circleAlert` icon, error message, "Try Again" retry button, and "Go Home" dismiss button. Gracefully handles 404 (recommendation not found) and network errors. (3) **Content** — `ScrollView` containing a `RecommendationCard` (reused for visual consistency) with data mapped from `MilestoneRecommendationItemResponse`. Currency hardcoded to "USD" (not stored in DB). Save/Share are no-op for MVP. "Select" opens the external merchant URL via `MerchantHandoffService` (Step 9.3). "Go Home" button below the card dismisses to the Home screen. Uses `NavigationStack` with close button (Lucide `x`) and "Recommendation" title. **Step 9.4:** Manages its own return-to-app state via local `@State` properties (`pendingHandoffRecommendation: MilestoneRecommendationItemResponse?`, `showPurchasePromptSheet: Bool`) rather than through `RecommendationsViewModel`, keeping the deep link flow self-contained. `@Environment(\.scenePhase)` detects `background → active` transitions and calls `handleReturnFromMerchant()` (500ms delay). `openExternalURL()` sets `pendingHandoffRecommendation = rec` before calling `MerchantHandoffService`. Purchase prompt sheet wired via `.sheet(isPresented: $showPurchasePromptSheet)` presenting `PurchasePromptSheet`. "Yes" records `"purchased"` feedback via service (fire-and-forget). "Save for later" records `"saved"` feedback via service (no SwiftData context available in deep link view). Both clear pending state and provide haptic feedback. |

##### `Saved/` — Saved Recommendations Tab
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `SavedView.swift` | **Active (Step 16.1).** Saved tab showing all bookmarked recommendations from SwiftData. `NavigationStack` with "Saved" title and `Theme.backgroundGradient`. Three states: (1) **Empty** — Lucide `bookmark` icon + "No saved items" message + guidance text. (2) **Content** — `ScrollView` of `savedRecommendationCard()` components (each with type SF Symbol icon, title, merchant name, formatted price via `RecommendationCard.formattedPrice()`, external link button, delete button). Data loaded via `SavedViewModel.loadSavedRecommendations(modelContext:)` in `.task`. No item limit (unlike the previous 5-item HomeView section). **Step 18.18:** Migrated the data load from `.onAppear` to `.task` so the fetch runs after SwiftUI's first layout pass instead of during it, eliminating a hit-test stall on the first tap into the Saved tab on real devices. |
| `SavedViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 16.1).** `@Observable @MainActor` class managing saved recommendations data. `savedRecommendations: [SavedRecommendation]` array. `loadSavedRecommendations(modelContext:)` fetches all `SavedRecommendation` objects sorted by `savedAt` descending via `FetchDescriptor` (no `fetchLimit`). `deleteSavedRecommendation(_:modelContext:)` deletes from SwiftData and removes from local array. Extracted from `HomeViewModel` during tab navigation refactor. **Step 18.18:** `loadSavedRecommendations(modelContext:)` is now `async` with a `await Task.yield()` before the fetch. The yield lets SwiftUI complete its initial layout pass before the `ModelContext.fetch` runs, so the Saved tab feels tappable the moment it appears even with a large saved-items collection. |

##### `Notifications/` — Notification History Feature
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `NotificationsView.swift` | **Active (Step 7.7).** Full Notification History screen presented as a `.sheet` from the Home screen's bell icon. `NavigationStack` with `Theme.backgroundGradient`, "Notifications" title, X dismiss button (Lucide `x`). Three states: (1) **Loading** — centered `ProgressView` during initial `loadHistory()`. (2) **Empty** — Lucide `bellRing` icon + "No notifications yet" message + guidance text. (3) **Notifications list** — `List` of `notificationRow()` components (`.listStyle(.plain)`, transparent background, hidden separators). Each row shows: left: milestone type SF Symbol icon in accent-tinted rounded rect (gift.fill/heart.fill/star.fill/calendar.badge.clock); center: milestone name (bold, 1-line) + unviewed accent dot (7pt Circle when `viewedAt == nil && status == "sent"`), days-before label + formatted date (secondary), status capsule badge (`statusBadge()` — green "Delivered" or red "Failed" with checkmark/xmark SF Symbol), recommendation count with Lucide `sparkles` icon; right: Lucide `chevronRight` if has recommendations. Tapping a row with `recommendationsCount > 0` calls `viewModel.selectNotification()`. Pull-to-refresh via `.refreshable`. **Recommendations sheet:** `.sheet` bound to `viewModel.showRecommendationsSheet`. Contains `NavigationStack` with milestone name title, X dismiss button. Four sub-states: loading spinner, error (exclamationmark.triangle + message), empty (Lucide sparkles + "No recommendations"), content (`ScrollView` of `recommendationCard()` components). Each card: type icon (gift.fill/sparkles/heart.fill/star.fill) in accent-tinted rect, title (bold, 2-line), merchant name + formatted price (caption), description (3-line), "View Details" external link button (opens URL via `UIApplication.shared.open()`). `.task { await viewModel.loadHistory() }` on appear. `.alert` for error messages. All colors use Theme constants. |
| `NotificationsViewModel.swift` | **Active (Step 7.7).** `@Observable @MainActor final class` managing notification history state and recommendation detail. **History state:** `isLoading` (initial load), `notifications: [NotificationHistoryItemResponse]` (display data), `errorMessage: String?` (alert). **Detail state:** `selectedNotification: NotificationHistoryItemResponse?`, `isLoadingRecommendations` (spinner in sheet), `milestoneRecommendations: [MilestoneRecommendationItemResponse]` (recommendation cards), `showRecommendationsSheet: Bool`, `recommendationsError: String?`. **Methods:** `loadHistory()` calls `NotificationHistoryService.fetchHistory()` and populates `notifications` array. `selectNotification(_:)` sets selected notification, shows sheet, calls `fetchMilestoneRecommendations(milestoneId:)`, marks notification as viewed (fire-and-forget via `service.markViewed()`), and creates a copy of the notification with `viewedAt` set for immediate UI feedback (removes unviewed dot without reload). `dismissRecommendations()` resets all detail state. **Helpers:** `formattedDate(_:)` parses ISO 8601 (with/without fractional seconds) and returns medium date + short time; `daysBeforeLabel(_:)` returns "X days before"; `milestoneTypeIcon(_:)` maps type to SF Symbol; `formattedPrice(cents:currency:)` converts integer cents to locale-aware currency string via `NumberFormatter`. Dependency-injected `NotificationHistoryService` via init parameter. |

##### `Onboarding/` — Partner Vault Onboarding Flow
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `OnboardingViewModel.swift` | `@Observable @MainActor` class managing all onboarding state. Defines `CustomMilestone` struct (Identifiable, Sendable — name, month, day, recurrence), `HolidayOption` struct (Identifiable, Sendable — id, displayName, month, day, iconName; static `allHolidays` with 5 US holidays), and the `OnboardingStep` enum (**12 cases** — since **Step 18.35** the three per-tier budget steps were collapsed into a single `budget` step, since **Step 18.38** the `primaryLoveLanguage` and `secondaryLoveLanguage` steps were merged into one `loveLanguages` step, since **Step 18.40** the `holidays` step was removed entirely (all five predefined holidays are now seeded by default), and since **Step 18.41** the `budget` step was removed entirely (the three budget tiers are now seeded with default ranges): welcome → partnerName → tenure → cohabitation → location → interests → dislikes → birthday → anniversary → vibes → loveLanguages → completion). The enum exposes `title` (which groups sibling sub-steps under one category label — all four partner-info screens read "Partner Info", all four milestones screens read "Milestones", etc.), `isFirst`, `isLast`, and `totalSteps`. Holds `currentStep`, `progress` (0.0–1.0), `showsBackButton` (true from step 3 / Tenure onward, gating the header back button), `canProceed` flag, `validationMessage` (computed user-facing error or nil), and all data properties (partnerName, selectedInterests, selectedDislikes, selectedVibes, budget amounts, love languages, milestones incl. `customMilestones: [CustomMilestone]`). Provides `goToNextStep()`, `goToPreviousStep()`, `daysInMonth()` / `clampDay()` static date helpers, and `validateCurrentStep()` — a switch where each one-question step validates only its own input (`.partnerName` requires non-empty name, `.location` requires city + state, `.interests` requires exactly 5, `.dislikes` requires exactly 5 and disjoint from interests, `.vibes` requires ≥ 1, `.loveLanguages` (the merged primary + secondary step, since **Step 18.38**) requires both a primary and a secondary that differ, and — since **Step 18.32** — `.birthday` requires `hasSetBirthday` and `.anniversary` requires `!hasAnniversary || hasSetAnniversary` (the `hasSetBirthday` / `hasSetAnniversary` flags flip true only when the user saves a date in the `MilestoneDateModal`, so no date is silently auto-saved); since **Step 18.33** `.tenure` requires `hasSetTenure` (same pattern — flips true only when the user saves a length in the `RelationshipLengthModal`, so no default tenure is silently saved); all other steps default to true). `validationMessage` mirrors the same switch with step-specific user-facing strings. Navigation methods call `validateCurrentStep()` after every step change. Step views also call it via `.onAppear` / `.onChange` for real-time validation. Created by `OnboardingContainerView` and injected into environment — all step views share the same instance. **Step 18.40:** added `init(seedDefaultHolidays: Bool = false)` — onboarding passes `true` so `selectedHolidays` is pre-populated with every `HolidayOption.allHolidays` id (all five holidays become reminder milestones by default, no picker step); the Settings edit flow uses the default `false` and hydrates `selectedHolidays` from the backend, so seeding never leaks into editing. **Step 18.41:** the six budget property defaults (`justBecauseMin`…`majorMilestoneMax`) now seed Just Because $50–$150, Minor Occasion $125–$375, and Major Milestone $250–$750 (cents); with the `budget` step gone these defaults flow straight into `buildVaultPayload()` (still always emitting all three tiers) and are edited later in Settings → Edit Profile → Budget Tiers. |
| `OnboardingContainerView.swift` | Navigation shell for the 12-step onboarding flow (16 since **Step 18.35** merged the three budget steps into one; 15 since **Step 18.37** merged holidays + custom milestones into one `holidays` step; 13 since **Step 18.40** removed the `holidays` step entirely — holidays are now seeded by default and the container creates `OnboardingViewModel(seedDefaultHolidays: true)`; 12 since **Step 18.41** removed the `budget` step entirely — budget tiers are now seeded with default ranges). Owns `OnboardingViewModel` via `@State` and injects it into the SwiftUI environment. Displays: (1) animated progress bar at top with the current step's category title and "Step X of 12" counter, (2) current step view in center via `@ViewBuilder` switch (12 cases routing to the per-question views; the former `.budget` → `OnboardingBudgetView` route was removed in **Step 18.41** and the former `.holidays` → `OnboardingHolidaysMilestonesView` route was removed in **Step 18.40**), (3) validation error banner (red, slides up, auto-dismisses after 3s) when user taps Next on an invalid step, (4) Back/Next/Get Started buttons at bottom. All buttons use `.fixedSize(horizontal: true, vertical: false)` to prevent text wrapping. Next button is always tappable — when `canProceed` is false, it shows the error banner from `viewModel.validationMessage` instead of advancing; tint dims to 40% opacity as a visual hint. Back button hidden on first step; "Get Started" replaces "Next" on last step. Error banner auto-clears on step change. Uses `.id(viewModel.currentStep)` for step identity and `.transition(.asymmetric(...))` for slide animations. Accepts `onComplete` closure called when user finishes onboarding. **Step 18.17:** Outer `VStack` adds `.ignoresSafeArea(.keyboard, edges: .bottom)` so opening the keyboard on text-field steps (Partner Name, Location, Custom Milestones) no longer drags the full-width Next button up against the keyboard — the entire chrome stays anchored and the keyboard slides up over the bottom of the screen. The opposite call from `KnotTabBar` (which intentionally rides the keyboard since the hint-capture input is next to it), made because the onboarding text field is mid-screen and the Next CTA is far below. Each step's inner `ScrollView` still handles its own keyboard scrolling. **Step 18.18:** Moved `.animation(.easeInOut(duration: 0.25), value: viewModel.currentStep)` from the outer `VStack` down to `stepContent` only. The previous outer-scoped 0.3s animation propagated to the navigation buttons (their `.opacity(canProceed ? 1.0 : 0.4)` modifier animated through every step swap), which delayed first taps on the new step's Next button on real devices. Scoping the animation to the step content alone keeps the buttons hit-testable from the moment the new step appears. **Step 18.27:** The top progress tracker (step-category title + "Step X of 16" counter + animated bar) is now wrapped in `if !viewModel.currentStep.isFirst`, so it is hidden on the Welcome step (`OnboardingStep.welcome`) to match the Figma design (node 87:2) and re-appears on steps 2–16. The `progressBar` computed property and `OnboardingViewModel.progress` are unchanged; only the call site is gated. **Step 18.28:** The header is now an `HStack(spacing: 16) { backButton; progressBar }` (same `!isFirst` gate and padding), adding a back button to the left of the progress bar per the Figma design (node 107:4315) — this supersedes the older "bottom Back button" description above, which was never actually implemented. The `backButton` is conditionally inserted based on `viewModel.showsBackButton` (`currentStep.rawValue > OnboardingStep.partnerName.rawValue`): absent on Welcome and Partner Name (where the only step back is the Welcome intro) so the progress bar spans full width, and from step 3 (Tenure) onward it appears and pushes the progress bar right, shrinking its width. The header `HStack` is pinned to `.frame(height: KnotIconButton.Size.lg.diameter)` (with vertical centering) so the progress bar's Y position stays constant on every step regardless of the button — only its width changes. The width change is animated via `.transition(.move(edge: .leading).combined(with: .opacity))` on the button + `.animation(.easeInOut(duration: 0.25), value: showsBackButton)` on the header, keyed to `showsBackButton` so it fires only at the Partner Name ↔ Tenure boundary and never propagates to the nav buttons. The `backButton` computed view reuses `KnotIconButton` with the `.ghost` variant (accent-tinted `Lucide.chevronLeft`, `.lg` size — 48pt tap target / 24pt glyph, `.padding(.leading, -10)` to align the glyph to the 24pt margin) wired to `viewModel.goToPreviousStep()`. A `@State isNavigatingBack` flag makes the `stepContent` slide transition direction-aware (back nav slides in from leading / out to trailing); it is set in each navigation action site (true on back, false on Next). **Step 18.42:** vault submission moved off the (deleted) summary step onto the **Love Languages** step — its "Next" button now `await viewModel.submitVault()` then `goToNextStep()` on success (the `isSubmitting` overlay covers the POST; the "Unable to Save" alert retries on failure, also advancing via `goToNextStep()`). `navigationButtons` is now three branches: `.isLast` (the `.completion` reveal) shows a "Continue" button calling `onComplete()` directly (always enabled/visible so the user is never trapped in a loading/error state); `.loveLanguages` runs the submit-then-advance flow; all other steps unchanged. The shared validation-banner logic was extracted into a `presentValidationError()` helper. The header row is now additionally gated on `viewModel.showsProgressHeader` (`currentStep != .completion`) so the back button + "Step X of 12" disappear on the reveal step. **Step 18.44:** vault submission moved off this view entirely — onto the reveal step (`OnboardingCompletionView`) — so a single `ForYouLoadingView` covers both vault creation and recommendation generation. The `isSubmitting` `KnotProgressIndicator.Overlay` ("Creating your partner vault…") and the "Unable to Save" submission-error alert were removed, and the dedicated `.loveLanguages` nav-button branch was deleted (it now falls through to the generic "Next" branch, which just calls `goToNextStep()` after the `canProceed` check). `navigationButtons` is now two branches: `.isLast` ("Continue") and everything else ("Next"/"Get Started"). |
