A single `select(_:)` applies the guided sequential rules: an unselected tap fills primary first then secondary; tapping the PRIMARY card promotes the secondary up to primary (keeping badges contiguous); tapping the SECONDARY card clears it. Validation (`.loveLanguages`) requires both set and different. |
| `OnboardingCompletionView.swift` | 12 | **Active (Step 3.9, fully rewritten Step 18.42).** The final onboarding step, now an **in-onboarding recommendation reveal** (the static "You're All Set!" partner-profile summary it used to render — 6 `SummaryCard` sections — was deleted). By the time it appears the vault has already been submitted (the Love Languages step's "Next" button POSTs it), so its `.task` calls `viewModel.configure(modelContext:)` + `viewModel.generateRecommendations()` on a fresh `@State RecommendationsViewModel` — the default args generate a `"just_because"` trio (the same run `JustBecauseCard` makes). State switch mirrors `RecommendationsView.suggestionsContent`: `viewModel.isLoading` → `ForYouLoadingView`; `isPlayingClimax` (driven by the same `.onChange(of: viewModel.isLoading)` celebration trigger) → `ForYouClimaxView`; `errorMessage` → message + "Try Again" (re-calls `generateRecommendations()`); empty → reassurance copy; loaded → an `OnboardingStepHeader("Here are your first picks", …)` over a `ScrollView`/`LazyVStack(spacing: 16)` of `RecommendationCard`s. The card CTAs match the For You tab: `onSelect` routes ideas/plans → `viewModel.openIdeaFromTrio` and gifts/experiences → `viewModel.selectRecommendation`, and the return-to-app handoff modifiers from `RecommendationsView` are ported onto `body` (`SelectionConfirmationSheet`, `IdeaDetailView` fullScreenCover, `PurchasePromptSheet`, `PurchaseRatingSheet`, and the `@Environment(\.scenePhase)` `handleReturnFromMerchant` detection); `onSave` calls `viewModel.saveRecommendation`. Deliberately omits the `RecommendationsView` *chrome* that doesn't belong here — the toolbar, the 100pt tab-bar bottom clearance (uses 24pt), the Adjust Vibe / Refresh buttons, and the `vaultMissing → hasCompletedOnboarding = false` re-route (a read-after-write lag could otherwise bounce the user out of onboarding mid-reveal) — and also omits two For-You behaviors that are premature during first-run onboarding: the App Store review prompt (`AppReviewPromptSheet` / `requestReview`) and the background "still preparing" notification (`handleAppBackgroundedWhileLoading`). The "Continue" button that finishes onboarding lives in the container's navigation bar (always reachable in every state). **Step 18.44:** vault submission moved *into* this view so a single `ForYouLoadingView` covers both vault creation and recommendation generation (the prior "Creating your partner vault…" overlay on the container was removed). Adds `@Environment(OnboardingViewModel.self) private var onboarding` plus `vaultReady`/`vaultFailed` state; the `.task` now runs `submitVaultThenGenerate()` — `await onboarding.submitVault()`, then on success set `vaultReady` immediately before `await viewModel.generateRecommendations()` (so the loading screen never flashes the empty state), or set `vaultFailed`. The state switch shows `ForYouLoadingView` while `!vaultReady || viewModel.isLoading`, and a vault-failure branch reuses `errorState` (now parameterized with a `retry` closure) showing `onboarding.submissionError` + "Try Again" that re-runs the flow; the generation-error branch passes its own retry. `#Preview` injects `.environment(OnboardingViewModel())`. |

Flat layout: a tinted leading icon chip (`RoundedRectangle` radius 10, `Theme.accent.opacity(0.20)` selected else `white.opacity(0.08)`), a leading `VStack` of the title (`Theme.Typography.cta`, `Theme.textPrimary`) plus, when a non-empty `subtitle` is supplied, a secondary line (`Theme.Typography.label`, `Theme.textSecondary`), and a trailing `checkmark.circle.fill` only when selected. **Step 18.34:** added the optional, defaulted `subtitle: String? = nil` so vibe rows can show their description; interests/dislikes pass no subtitle and render title-only as before. | `AnimatedCoupleIllustration.swift` | **Step 18.26.** Idle animation wrapping the `onboarding-0` couple illustration, ported from a Figma Make (Framer Motion) prototype to native SwiftUI. A `ZStack` of three infinitely-looping ambient layers: (1) couple **float + breathe** (`offset(y:)` 0↔−10, `scaleEffect` 1.0↔1.018, 4s cycle via `.repeatForever(autoreverses:)`); (2) a blurred `RadialGradient` `Ellipse` **glow pulse** anchored to `Theme.colorPrimary.opacity(0.18)` (opacity 0.25↔0.45, scale 0.97↔1.03, 5s); (3) six `FloatingHeart` views (private) each driven by `keyframeAnimator(initialValue:repeating:)` over the prototype's multi-stop path (opacity/y/x-drift/scale at `times [0,0.1,0.35,0.7,1]`), with per-heart `delay` applied once via an `.onAppear` start gate. Private `HeartShape: Shape` transcribes the prototype's SVG heart path; six rose shades are local constants derived from the brand coral. `static let heartConfigs` exposes the six configs for tests. Honors `accessibilityReduceMotion` by falling back to the static `Image`. Native SwiftUI only — no Lottie/Rive. Consumed by `OnboardingWelcomeView`. Tested in `AnimatedCoupleIllustrationTests`. |

The cover's bottom-slide is disabled (present/dismiss inside a `disablesAnimations` `Transaction`); the backdrop fades and the card independently scales (0.94→1.0)+fades on a smooth spring on appear, easing out via `animateOut(then:)` on dismiss. #### `/Core` — Shared Utilities
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `Constants.swift` | App-wide constants: API URLs, Supabase configuration (`projectURL`, `anonKey`), validation rules, predefined categories (40 interests, 8 vibes, 5 love languages). **Step 19.0:** the DEBUG `API.baseURL` is no longer a hardcoded literal — it resolves via `resolveDebugBaseURL(override:injected:)` in priority order: `UserDefaults["KnotDevAPIBaseURL"]` manual override → `DevServer.plist[DevAPIBaseURL]` (the Mac's LAN IP auto-injected at build time by `iOS/scripts/inject-dev-host.sh`) → `http://127.0.0.1:8000` fallback. This lets the simulator and a physical iPhone both reach the local backend with zero manual edits; source keeps only the loopback fallback (never commit a LAN IP). Release path (`https://api.knot-app.com`) unchanged. |
| `DeepLinkHandler.swift` | **Active (Step 9.2).** `@Observable @MainActor` class managing deep link state for Universal Links. Defines `DeepLinkDestination` enum (currently `.recommendation(id: String)`, extensible for future deep link types). `handleURL(_:)` parses incoming Universal Link URLs by splitting the path into components and matching against known patterns (`/recommendation/{id}`). Sets `pendingDestination: DeepLinkDestination?` which `HomeView` observes via `.onChange` (warm start) and `.task` (cold start) to trigger navigation. After consuming, the view clears `pendingDestination = nil`. Unrecognized paths are silently ignored (logged to console). Created as `@State` in `KnotApp` and injected into the SwiftUI environment. Follows the same `@Observable @MainActor` pattern as `AuthViewModel` and `NetworkMonitor`. |
| `NetworkMonitor.swift` | **Active (Step 4.1, updated Step 16.1).** `@Observable @MainActor` class monitoring network connectivity via `NWPathMonitor` (from `Network` framework). Publishes `isConnected: Bool` updated on the main actor when the network path changes. Creates a dedicated `DispatchQueue` for the monitor's `pathUpdateHandler`. Starts monitoring immediately on `init()`, cancels on `deinit`. **Step 16.1:** Hoisted from `HomeView` `@State` to `MainTabView` `@State` and injected via `.environment()` so all tabs can access connectivity state. `HomeView` now reads it via `@Environment(NetworkMonitor.self)`. |
| `LocationSearchCompleter.swift` | **Active (Step 3.13).** `@Observable @MainActor` wrapper around `MKLocalSearchCompleter` providing address autocomplete for the onboarding location field. Configures `resultTypes = .address` to filter out POIs. `search(query:)` updates `queryFragment` and populates `results: [MKLocalSearchCompletion]` via delegate callbacks. `resolve(_:)` performs an async `MKLocalSearch` to extract structured `selectedCity` (locality), `selectedState` (administrativeArea), and `selectedZip` (postalCode) from the first placemark. Falls back to completion title/subtitle on error. Delegate methods use `nonisolated(unsafe)` to bridge non-Sendable `MKLocalSearchCompletion` into `@MainActor` tasks for Swift 6 strict concurrency compliance. No location permissions required — MapKit search works without them. |
| `Theme.swift` | **App-wide design system (Step 3.3).** Centralizes all colors, gradients, and surfaces for the dark purple aesthetic. Contains: `backgroundGradient` (dark purple LinearGradient from `(0.10, 0.05, 0.16)` to `(0.05, 0.02, 0.10)`), `surface` / `surfaceElevated` / `surfaceBorder` (semi-transparent white at 8%/12%/12% opacity), `accent` (Color.pink), `textPrimary` / `textSecondary` / `textTertiary` (white at 100%/60%/35% opacity), and `progressTrack` / `progressFill`. All views MUST use `Theme` constants — never hardcode colors. **Step 18.1:** Added four nested token namespaces consumed by `Components/UI/` primitives — `Theme.Spacing` (4pt grid: xxs/xs/sm/md/lg/xl/xxl/xxxl), `Theme.Radius` (sm=8 / md=12 / lg=14 / xl=18 / pill=999; `lg` matches the dominant corner-radius across the codebase, `xl` matches `RecommendationCard`), `Theme.Typography` (semantic font tokens xs/sm/base/body/lg/xl/xxl/display), and `Theme.Motion` (animation curves `standard` / `quick`). **Step 18.8:** Added three more foundation families. Status colors `statusError` / `statusSuccess` / `statusWarning` / `statusInfo` plus matching pre-baked 12%-alpha `*Tint` variants (8 tokens total) — adaptive light/dark via `UIColor { tc in ... }`, replacing raw `Color.red` / `Color.green` literals across `KnotBadge`, `KnotButton`, and `KnotInput`. Shadow tokens via `Theme.ShadowToken` struct + `Theme.Shadow` enum (`sm` / `md` / `lg` / `accentGlow`) plus a `View.shadow(_ token:)` extension so callers write `.shadow(Theme.Shadow.md)` instead of four loose params; values are derived from existing chip and card shadow patterns. `Theme.Weight` enum aliasing `Font.Weight` for `regular` / `medium` / `semibold` / `bold` / `heavy` (deliberately excludes `.thin` / `.ultraLight` / `.black`). Existing color tokens unchanged. **Step 18.20:** Converted `backgroundGradient` from `static var` (computed property — allocates a new `LinearGradient` on every access) to `static let` (allocated once at app load). Every major view applies `Theme.backgroundGradient.ignoresSafeArea()` as its root background, so every view-body re-evaluation was previously paying a fresh allocation. `backgroundTop` / `backgroundBottom` are themselves adaptive `Color(UIColor { tc in ... })` tokens, so light/dark trait changes still resolve correctly through the memoized gradient. **Step 18.10:** `Theme.Typography` rewritten for the **Fraunces + DM Sans** custom-font pairing. Eight semantic tokens — `heroDisplay` (Fraunces-Light 42pt, sign-in wordmark), `sectionHeader` (Fraunces-Light 28pt, page titles), `cardTitle` (Fraunces-Regular 20pt, secondary headings), `italicQuote` (Fraunces-LightItalic 17pt, brand-moment italics), `body` (DMSans-Regular 17pt, default copy), `label` (DMSans-Medium 13pt, captions), `cta` (DMSans-SemiBold 17pt, buttons), `numeric` (DMSans-Bold 17pt, counts/streaks). Each token is built via `Font.custom(_:size:relativeTo:)` so it scales with iOS Dynamic Type relative to a matched system style. A `private enum FontFamily` holds the 7 PostScript-name string constants. The 8 legacy token names (`xs` … `display`) remain as `@available(*, deprecated)` typealiases mapping to the closest new token. `Theme.Weight` is now `@available(*, deprecated)` end-to-end — weight is baked into each Typography token, and chaining `.fontWeight(...)` after a custom-font token can re-substitute the system font on some iOS versions. New `View.knotFont(_ token: Font)` extension is the single migration entry point (it intentionally does not chain `.fontWeight(...)`); a `Text.knotFont(_:)` overload exists for `Text + Text` concatenation cases (sign-in wordmark, magic-link confirmation). New `Theme.registerFonts()` debug helper prints `UIFont.familyNames` and per-family `fontNames` for `"Fraunces"` and `"DM Sans"` under `#if DEBUG` — the only reliable signal that bundle registration succeeded since `Font.custom` silently falls back to the system font when a face isn't bundled. Called once from `KnotApp.init()`. Custom font files live at `iOS/Knot/Resources/Fonts/` (auto-bundled by XcodeGen via `sources: [path: Knot]`) and are listed in `Info.plist` `UIAppFonts`. Both Fraunces and DM Sans are SIL OFL 1.1 licensed (commercial embedding allowed, no in-app attribution required). **Step 18.21:** Added a `MARK: - Brand Palette` section between `Accent` and `Text` with three new adaptive tokens — `colorPrimary` (coral-pink, matches `signInButtonPrimary` in light; same hue in dark since it already reads as a brand mark on the deep-purple background), `colorSecondary` (warm cream `rgb(1.0, 0.94, 0.88)` in light = `signInCream`; warm-tinted dark `rgb(0.18, 0.13, 0.12)` in dark, preserving the "soft supporting surface" semantic rather than forcing a cream fill onto the dark gradient), and `colorTertiary` (deep plum `rgb(0.12, 0.10, 0.16)` in light = `textPrimary` light; off-white `rgb(0.95, 0.93, 0.95)` in dark, mirroring how `textPrimary` itself inverts). Each token is `Color(UIColor { tc in ... })` so trait changes resolve automatically. Existing role-specific tokens (`signInButtonPrimary`, `signInCream`, `accent`) were intentionally left in place — they carry sign-in-specific or system-color semantics that would be lost by collapsing them into the brand palette. New surfaces should prefer the brand palette tokens; existing sign-in call sites stay on their role-specific tokens. Locked in `ThemeTokensTests` via an `assertRGB(_:in:equals:name:)` helper that resolves each `Color` through `UIColor.resolvedColor(with:)` and asserts per-channel floats within `0.005` accuracy across both trait collections. **Step 18.22:** Added `Theme.Typography.onboardingHeader` — Fraunces (variable font, `.weight(.semibold)`) @ 32pt scaling relative to `.title` (was 28pt at introduction; bumped to 32pt in Step 18.25 after the welcome-screen redesign validated the larger size on every onboarding header). Sister token to `sectionHeader`: identical family and Dynamic Type relation; only the variable-axis weight (`.semibold` vs `.light`) and size (32pt vs 28pt) differ. Reserved for onboarding page titles so the onboarding flow reads heavier and more deliberate without disturbing the ~15 non-onboarding `sectionHeader` call sites (Auth, Settings, Home, Recommendations). Weight is baked into the token at definition time rather than chained as `.fontWeight(...)` at the call site — chaining `.fontWeight(...)` after `.knotFont(...)` can cause iOS to silently fall back to the system font. Migrated 10 onboarding step views (`OnboardingWelcomeView`, `OnboardingVibesView`, `OnboardingDislikesView`, `OnboardingInterestsView`, `OnboardingPrimaryLoveLanguageView`, `OnboardingSecondaryLoveLanguageView`, `OnboardingMinorOccasionBudgetView`, `OnboardingJustBecauseBudgetView`, `OnboardingMajorMilestoneBudgetView`, `OnboardingCompletionView`); `cardTitle`-based onboarding headers (Birthday, PartnerName, Anniversary, Holidays, Location, Cohabitation, Tenure, CustomMilestones) intentionally left on `cardTitle` since that token carries an app-wide "secondary heading" semantic. Locked in `ThemeTokensTests` via `testOnboardingHeaderTokenExists`. **Step 18.23:** Added `Theme.Typography.onboardingSubHeader` — Fraunces (variable font, `.weight(.semibold)`) @ 20pt scaling relative to `.title2`. Sister token to `cardTitle`: identical family, size, and Dynamic Type relation; only the variable-axis weight differs (`.semibold` vs `.regular`). Paired with `onboardingHeader` (28pt) from Step 18.22 to give the onboarding flow a consistent semibold treatment at two scales — `onboardingHeader` for the 10 informational page titles, `onboardingSubHeader` for the 8 form-style page titles (Birthday, Anniversary, PartnerName, CustomMilestones, Holidays, Location, Cohabitation, Tenure) where the header sits above a date picker, toggle, or text field. The inline form-field labels on Birthday and Anniversary (the "Birthday" / "Anniversary" labels next to their respective inputs) intentionally stay on `cardTitle` since they are not page headers; the visible weight contrast between page header and field label is the proof point. ~20 non-onboarding `cardTitle` call sites and the shared `BudgetTierCard` / `LoveLanguageCard` / `VibeCard` internals are untouched. Locked in `ThemeTokensTests` via `testOnboardingSubHeaderTokenExists`. **Step 18.25:** All 8 `onboardingSubHeader` call sites (`OnboardingBirthdayView`, `OnboardingAnniversaryView`, `OnboardingPartnerNameView`, `OnboardingTenureView`, `OnboardingCohabitationView`, `OnboardingLocationView`, `OnboardingHolidaysView`, `OnboardingCustomMilestonesView`) were migrated to `onboardingHeader` so every one of the 18 onboarding pages uses the same 32pt page title. The `onboardingSubHeader` token itself is left in `Theme.swift` and its existence test is left passing — it's currently dead but cheap to keep around if a smaller onboarding title scale is ever wanted again; a follow-up cleanup pass can delete it if it stays unused. Inline field labels on Birthday/Anniversary that use `cardTitle` (20pt) are untouched. **Step 18.55:** Added `Theme.Typography.bodySmall` — `DMSans-Regular @ 16pt, relativeTo: .body` — sitting in the ramp between `label` (13) and `body` (17). Consumed by `RecommendationDetailView`'s stacked meta row (merchant/price/location) and its "Why Knot picked this" personalization note (which moved off `italicQuote` to match the Figma at node 157-189). |

Future files:
- `Extensions.swift` — Swift type extensions

#### `/Services` — Data & API Layer
| File | Status | Purpose |
|------|--------|---------|
| `SupabaseClient.swift` | **Active** | Singleton `SupabaseManager.client` initialized with `Constants.Supabase.projectURL` and `anonKey`. The Supabase Swift SDK automatically handles Keychain session storage and token refresh. Used by `AuthViewModel`, `VaultService`, and future service classes. |
| `VaultService.swift` | **Active (Step 3.12)** | `@MainActor` service for Partner Vault API operations. Four methods: (1) `createVault(_:)` — sends `POST /api/v1/vault` with full onboarding payload; handles 201 success, 401 auth, 409 duplicate, 422 validation, and network errors with typed `VaultServiceError` enum. (2) `getVault()` — sends `GET /api/v1/vault` to retrieve full vault data (all 6 tables); handles 200 success, 401 auth, 404 not found. Returns `VaultGetResponse`. (3) `updateVault(_:)` — sends `PUT /api/v1/vault` with full vault payload (same schema as create); handles 200 success, 401 auth, 404 not found, 422 validation. Returns `VaultUpdateResponse`. (4) `vaultExists()` — queries Supabase PostgREST directly (`partner_vaults?select=id&limit=1`) using the anon client (RLS-scoped); returns `Bool`. All HTTP methods use Bearer token auth via `getAccessToken()`, `URLSession.shared`, `JSONEncoder`/`JSONDecoder`, and differentiate network errors by `URLError.code`. Called by `OnboardingViewModel.submitVault()`, `AuthViewModel.listenForAuthChanges()`, and `EditVaultView`. |
| `APIClient.swift` | Planned | Generic HTTP client for backend API calls (future refactor) |
| `HintService.swift` | **Active (Step 4.6, callers updated in Step 18.6)** | `@MainActor` service for Hint Capture API operations. Three methods: (1) `createHint(text:source:)` — sends `POST /api/v1/hints` with hint text and source ("text_input" or "voice_transcription"); handles 201 success, 401 auth, 404 no vault, 422 validation (empty text, text too long), and network errors with typed `HintServiceError` enum (6 cases mirroring `VaultServiceError` pattern). (2) `listHints(limit:offset:)` — sends `GET /api/v1/hints?limit=N&offset=M` to retrieve hints in reverse chronological order; handles 200 success, 401 auth, 404 no vault. Returns `HintListResponse`. (3) `deleteHint(id:)` — sends `DELETE /api/v1/hints/{id}` to permanently delete a hint; handles 204 success, 401 auth, 404 not found (hint doesn't exist or belongs to another user). Uses Bearer token auth via `getAccessToken()`, `URLSession.shared`, `JSONEncoder`/`JSONDecoder`, `mapURLError()` for typed network error differentiation. Parses both FastAPI error formats (string detail + array detail). **Step 18.6 callers:** `RecommendationsViewModel.submitSessionHintAndRefresh()` (best-effort write inside the recommendation refresh flow), and `SettingsViewModel.clearAllHints()` (uses `listHints` + `deleteHint` for the "Clear All Hints" action). The previous Home-screen and standalone-tab capture surfaces were removed in Step 18.6 along with their callers (`HomeViewModel.submitHint`/`loadRecentHints`, `HintsListViewModel.loadHints`/`deleteHint`). |
| `RecommendationService.swift` | **Active (Step 9.4)** | `@MainActor` service for Recommendation API operations. Four methods: (1) `generateRecommendations(occasionType:milestoneId:)` — sends `POST /api/v1/recommendations/generate` with occasion type and optional milestone ID; handles 200 success, 401 auth, 404 no vault, 422 validation, and network errors with typed `RecommendationServiceError` enum (7 cases including `.notFound`). Returns `RecommendationGenerateResponse`. (2) `refreshRecommendations(rejectedIds:reason:)` — sends `POST /api/v1/recommendations/refresh` with rejected recommendation IDs and rejection reason for exclusion filtering; same error handling. Returns `RecommendationRefreshResponse`. Both methods use 60-second timeout (longer than HintService's 30s) because the LangGraph AI pipeline involves multiple agent nodes. (3) **Step 6.3/9.4:** `recordFeedback(recommendationId:action:rating:feedbackText:)` — sends `POST /api/v1/recommendations/feedback`; marked `@discardableResult` for fire-and-forget usage; 15-second timeout; expects 201 status code. `rating: Int?` and `feedbackText: String?` optional params (default nil) added in Step 9.4 for post-purchase rating. Valid actions: "selected", "saved", "shared", "rated", "handoff", "purchased", "disliked" (Step 18.43 — the Spotlight deck's 👎). Returns `RecommendationFeedbackResponse`. (4) **Step 9.2:** `fetchRecommendation(id:)` — sends `GET /api/v1/recommendations/{id}` to fetch a single recommendation by database ID; 15-second timeout; handles 200 success, 401 auth, 404 `.notFound`. Returns `MilestoneRecommendationItemResponse`. Used by `DeepLinkRecommendationView` for Universal Link deep linking. Uses Bearer token auth via `getAccessToken()`, `URLSession.shared`, `JSONEncoder`/`JSONDecoder`, `parseErrorMessage()` for both FastAPI error formats. Called by `RecommendationsViewModel` and `DeepLinkRecommendationView`. |
| `NotificationHistoryService.swift` | **Active (Step 7.7)** | `@MainActor final class: Sendable` service for notification history API operations. Three methods: (1) `fetchHistory(limit:offset:)` — sends `GET /api/v1/notifications/history` with pagination params; handles 200 success, 401 auth, and generic server errors with typed `NotificationHistoryServiceError` enum (4 cases: noAuthSession, networkError, serverError, decodingError). Returns `NotificationHistoryResponse`. (2) `fetchMilestoneRecommendations(milestoneId:)` — sends `GET /api/v1/recommendations/by-milestone/{milestoneId}`; handles 200, 401, 404, server errors. Returns `MilestoneRecommendationsResponse`. (3) `markViewed(notificationId:)` — sends `PATCH /api/v1/notifications/{notificationId}/viewed`; fire-and-forget (catches all errors, logs to console, never throws). Uses Bearer token auth via `getAccessToken()` from `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session`. Follows `RecommendationService.swift` patterns: `mapURLError()` for typed `URLError` differentiation, `parseErrorMessage()` for both FastAPI error formats (string detail + array detail). 15-second timeout for fetch operations, 10-second for mark-viewed. Called by `NotificationsViewModel`. |
| `AccountService.swift` | **Active (Step 15.6)** | `@MainActor final class: Sendable` service for account-lifecycle API operations. Public methods: (1) `deleteAccount() async throws` — sends `DELETE /api/v1/users/me`; backend responds 200 with `AccountDeleteResponse` (`status="scheduled"`, `scheduled_deletion_at` ISO timestamp). (2) `restoreAccount() async throws` — sends `POST /api/v1/users/me/restore` to clear `scheduled_deletion_at`; idempotent on the server. (3) `fetchAccountStatus() async throws -> AccountStatus` — sends `GET /api/v1/users/me` and returns `.active` or `.pendingDeletion(scheduledAt: Date)`. Used by `AuthViewModel.refreshPendingDeletionStatus()` to drive the `PendingDeletionView` gate. (4) `devResetForOnboarding() async throws` (Step 15.6) — sends `POST /api/v1/users/me/dev-reset`; backend wipes `partner_vaults` (CASCADE removes children) and clears `scheduled_deletion_at`. Method is always compiled (no `#if DEBUG` fence on the service) but every call site is fenced. Server returns 403 unless `KNOT_DEV_RESET_ENABLED=true`, surfaced as `AccountServiceError.serverError(statusCode: 403, ...)`. The `AccountStatus` enum is declared in this file. `parseISODate(_:)` static helper tolerates both fractional-second and basic ISO 8601 formats (Python `datetime.isoformat()` includes microseconds). Error enum: `AccountServiceError` with `.noAuthSession`, `.networkError(String)`, `.serverError(statusCode: Int, message: String)`. 30-second timeout, Bearer auth from `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session`. |
| `ExportService.swift` | **Active (Step 11.3)** | `@MainActor final class: Sendable` service for user data export API operations. Follows `AccountService.swift` pattern exactly. One public method: `exportData() async throws -> Data` — sends `GET /api/v1/users/me/export` with Bearer token auth from Supabase session, expects 200 response, returns the raw response `Data` (not decoded into a model). The raw Data is returned so the ViewModel can pretty-print it with `JSONSerialization` and write it to a temp file for sharing. Error enum: `ExportServiceError` with 3 cases (`.noAuthSession` — no active Supabase session, `.networkError(String)` — URL/connectivity failure, `.serverError(statusCode:message:)` — non-200 HTTP response with status code and parsed error message). Private helpers: `getAccessToken()` from `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session`, `mapURLError(_:)` for typed `URLError` differentiation, `parseErrorMessage(from:)` for both FastAPI error formats (string detail + array detail). 30-second timeout. Called by `SettingsViewModel.exportUserData()`. |
| `NotificationPreferencesService.swift` | **Active (Step 11.4)** | `@MainActor final class: Sendable` service for notification preferences API operations. Follows `ExportService.swift` pattern. Two public methods: (1) `fetchPreferences() async throws -> NotificationPreferencesDTO` — sends `GET /api/v1/users/me/notification-preferences` with Bearer token auth, decodes response into `NotificationPreferencesDTO`. (2) `updatePreferences(_ request: NotificationPreferencesUpdateDTO) async throws -> NotificationPreferencesDTO` — sends `PUT /api/v1/users/me/notification-preferences` with partial update payload, returns updated preferences. Error enum: `NotificationPreferencesServiceError` with 3 cases (`.noAuthSession`, `.networkError(String)`, `.serverError(statusCode:message:)`). Private helpers: `getAccessToken()`, `mapURLError(_:)`, `parseErrorMessage(from:)`. 30-second timeout. Called by `SettingsViewModel.loadNotificationPreferences()` and `SettingsViewModel.saveQuietHours()`. |
| `DeviceTokenService.swift` | **Active (Step 7.4)** | `@MainActor final class: Sendable` singleton for registering APNs device tokens with the backend. Uses `static let shared` because `AppDelegate.didRegisterForRemoteNotificationsWithDeviceToken` fires before the SwiftUI view hierarchy exists, making environment injection unavailable. One public method: `registerToken(_ token: String) async` — best-effort, catches all errors and logs them without surfacing to the user. Internally calls `sendToken()` which builds a `POST /api/v1/users/device-token` request with Bearer auth from Supabase session, sends `DeviceTokenPayload` (token + "ios" platform), and checks HTTP 200 response. Follows `HintService.swift` patterns: `getAccessToken()` from `SupabaseManager.client.auth.session`, `mapURLError()` for typed `URLError` differentiation, `parseErrorMessage()` for backend error response parsing. Error enum: `DeviceTokenServiceError` with 3 cases (noAuthSession, networkError, serverError). 30-second timeout. Called by `AppDelegate` on every app launch after successful APNs registration. |
| `MilestoneService.swift` | **Active (Step 17.1)** | `@MainActor` service for milestone CRUD API operations. Four methods: `listMilestones()` (GET), `createMilestone(_:)` (POST), `updateMilestone(id:_:)` (PUT), `deleteMilestone(id:)` (DELETE). Follows `RecommendationService` patterns with Bearer token auth, typed error enum, and `URLSession.shared`. Called by `MilestonesViewModel`. |
| `MerchantHandoffService.swift` | **Active (Step 9.3)** | `@MainActor enum` with a single static method `openMerchantURL(urlString:recommendationId:service:)` for external merchant handoff. Opens merchant URLs using a two-step strategy: (1) tries `UIApplication.shared.open(url, options: [.universalLinksOnly: true])` to prefer the merchant's native app if installed, (2) if that returns `false`, falls back to `UIApplication.shared.open(url)` which opens in Safari. After opening, records a `"handoff"` feedback action via `RecommendationService.recordFeedback()` (fire-and-forget `Task { }`). Returns `false` for invalid/empty URLs, `true` for valid ones. Injectable `service` parameter for testability. Called by `RecommendationsViewModel.confirmSelection()` and `DeepLinkRecommendationView.openExternalURL()`. |

#### `/Models` — Data Models
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `SyncStatus.swift` | Shared enum (`synced`, `pendingUpload`, `pendingDownload`) tracking local-to-Supabase sync state. Used by all `@Model` classes. Stored as raw `String` in SwiftData with a computed property for type-safe access. |
| `PartnerVaultLocal.swift` | SwiftData `@Model` mirroring `partner_vaults` table. Stores partner profile (name, tenure, cohabitation, location) locally. `remoteID` is nullable (NULL until synced with Supabase). |
| `HintLocal.swift` | SwiftData `@Model` mirroring `hints` table. Stores captured hints (text, source, isUsed). Deliberately excludes `hint_embedding` (vector(768)) — embeddings are server-side only for semantic search. |
| `MilestoneLocal.swift` | SwiftData `@Model` mirroring `partner_milestones` table. Stores milestones (type, name, date, recurrence, budgetTier) for Home screen countdown display. |
| `RecommendationLocal.swift` | SwiftData `@Model` mirroring `recommendations` table. Stores AI-generated recommendations for Choice-of-Three display. `description` renamed to `descriptionText` to avoid Swift protocol conflict. |
| `SavedRecommendation.swift` | **Active (Step 6.6).** SwiftData `@Model` for locally persisted saved recommendations. Stores a snapshot of recommendation data at save time: `recommendationId` (backend ID for deduplication), `recommendationType` (gift/experience/date), `title`, `descriptionText` (nullable), `externalURL`, `priceCents` (nullable, in cents), `currency` (defaults "USD"), `merchantName` (nullable), `imageURL` (nullable), `savedAt` (defaults to `Date()`). Surfaced on Home screen in the "Saved" section. Registered in `KnotApp.swift` model container schema. |
| `DTOs.swift` | **Active (Step 6.3).** Codable data transfer objects for backend API communication. **Vault request payloads:** `VaultCreatePayload` (full onboarding/edit submission with snake_case `CodingKeys` matching backend Pydantic `VaultCreateRequest` — used for both POST and PUT), `MilestonePayload` (milestone_type, name, date as `"2000-MM-DD"`, recurrence, budget_tier nullable), `BudgetPayload` (occasion_type, min/max amounts in cents, currency), `LoveLanguagesPayload` (primary + secondary). **Vault POST response:** `VaultCreateResponse` (vault_id, partner_name, summary counts, love_languages dict). **Vault GET response (Step 3.12):** `VaultGetResponse` (full vault data — all basic info fields, interests/dislikes as `[String]`, milestones as `[MilestoneGetResponse]`, vibes as `[String]`, budgets as `[BudgetGetResponse]`, love_languages as `[LoveLanguageGetResponse]`), `MilestoneGetResponse` (id, type, name, date, recurrence, budget_tier), `BudgetGetResponse` (id, occasion_type, min/max amounts, currency), `LoveLanguageGetResponse` (language, priority). **Vault PUT response (Step 3.12):** `VaultUpdateResponse` (mirrors VaultCreateResponse — vault_id, partner_name, summary counts, love_languages dict). **Hint DTOs (Step 4.2):** `HintCreatePayload` (hint_text, source with snake_case CodingKeys), `HintCreateResponse` (id, hint_text, source, is_used, created_at), `HintListResponse` (hints array + total count), `HintItemResponse` (same fields as HintCreateResponse — single hint in list). **Recommendation DTOs (Step 6.2):** `RecommendationGeneratePayload` (milestoneId nullable, occasionType), `RecommendationRefreshPayload` (rejectedRecommendationIds array, rejectionReason), `RecommendationGenerateResponse` (recommendations array, count, milestoneId nullable, occasionType), `RecommendationRefreshResponse` (recommendations array, count, rejectionReason), `RecommendationItemResponse` (Codable + Sendable + Identifiable — id, recommendationType, title, description nullable, priceCents nullable, currency, externalUrl, imageUrl nullable, merchantName nullable, source, location nullable, interestScore, vibeScore, loveLanguageScore, finalScore), `RecommendationLocationResponse` (city/state/country/address all nullable). **Feedback DTOs (Step 6.3):** `RecommendationFeedbackPayload` (recommendationId, action with snake_case CodingKeys), `RecommendationFeedbackResponse` (id, recommendationId, action, createdAt with snake_case CodingKeys). **Device Token DTO (Step 7.4):** `DeviceTokenPayload` (deviceToken, platform with snake_case CodingKeys — request-only, no response DTO needed since the service only checks HTTP status). **Notification History DTOs (Step 7.7):** `NotificationHistoryResponse` (notifications: array + total: Int), `NotificationHistoryItemResponse` (Identifiable — id, milestoneId, milestoneName, milestoneType, milestoneDate, daysBefore, status, sentAt nullable, viewedAt nullable, createdAt, recommendationsCount; CodingKeys for snake_case), `MilestoneRecommendationsResponse` (recommendations: array + count: Int + milestoneId), `MilestoneRecommendationItemResponse` (Identifiable — id, recommendationType, title, description nullable, externalUrl nullable, priceCents nullable, merchantName nullable, imageUrl nullable, createdAt; CodingKeys for snake_case). **Notification Preferences DTOs (Step 11.4):** `NotificationPreferencesDTO` (Codable + Sendable — notificationsEnabled: Bool, quietHoursStart: Int, quietHoursEnd: Int, timezone: String? with snake_case CodingKeys), `NotificationPreferencesUpdateDTO` (Codable + Sendable — all fields optional for partial updates with snake_case CodingKeys). All structs conform to `Codable` + `Sendable` with snake_case `CodingKeys`. |

#### `/Components` — Reusable UI Components
Layout helpers live at the root; shadcn-style design-system primitives live in `/Components/UI/`.

| File | Status | Purpose |
|------|--------|---------|
| `FlowLayout.swift` | **Active** | Custom `Layout` protocol implementation for wrapping flow (CSS `flex-wrap` equivalent). Arranges subviews left-to-right, wrapping to the next row when they exceed available width. Configurable `horizontalSpacing` and `verticalSpacing`. Created in Step 3.3 for chip grids; used by DislikesView (Step 3.4) and VibesView (Step 3.6). |

##### `/Components/UI` — shadcn-Style SwiftUI Primitives (Step 18.1, broader rollout in Step 18.2, `KnotTabBar` added in Step 18.3)
Native SwiftUI components in shadcn's aesthetic. Read tokens from `Theme` (colors, `Theme.Spacing`, `Theme.Radius`, `Theme.Typography`, `Theme.Motion`) — callers never pass colors. Closures are typed `@MainActor` for Swift 6 strict concurrency. **Step 18.2** fanned the primitive-based migration out across the rest of the production screens (RecommendationCard, HomeView, HintsListView, LoginView, OnboardingContainerView, OnboardingWelcomeView, OnboardingBudgetView, OnboardingCompletionView, OnboardingMilestonesView, EditVaultView). The four onboarding card screens (Interests, Dislikes, Vibes, LoveLanguages) and OnboardingBasicInfoView's text fields stayed inline as documented snowflakes — see Step 18.2 in `progress.md` for rationale. No new primitives were added in Phase 3; the original 8 covered every clean-fit migration. **Step 18.3** added a ninth primitive (`KnotTabBar`) when redesigning the bottom navigation to match Airbnb's mobile look — `UITabBar` cannot swap to filled-variant icons by selection state, so a SwiftUI primitive was the cleanest path.

| Component | Status | Purpose |
|-----------|--------|---------|
| `KnotCard.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Surface container with adaptive fill, 1pt border, rounded corners. Variants: `default`, `elevated`, `outlinedDashed`. Token-driven `Padding` (none/sm/md/lg/xl) and `Radius`. Foundation for every elevated container — domain cards (`RecommendationCard`, `JustBecauseCard`, etc.) compose this rather than rebuilding the chrome inline. |
| `KnotButton.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Generic `KnotButton<Label>` with shadcn variants (`primary`/`secondary`/`outline`/`ghost`/`destructive`), sizes (`sm`/`md`/`lg`), shapes (`rounded`/`pill`), built-in `isLoading` (swaps label for `ProgressView`), and Lucide `leadingIcon`/`trailingIcon`. Convenience init `KnotButton(_:variant:size:shape:isLoading:leadingIcon:trailingIcon:action:)` for plain text. Replaces `Capsule().fill(Theme.accent)` CTAs throughout the app. |
| `KnotIconButton.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Circular icon-only button. Variants: `primary` (pink fill), `surface` (toolbar-style with border), `ghost` (transparent). Sizes `sm`/`md`/`lg` (32/40/48 pt). Encapsulates the `renderingMode(.template) + resizable + frame` boilerplate. |
| `KnotBadge.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Pill-shaped label with semantic variants (`default`/`secondary`/`outline`/`accent`/`destructive`/`success`), sizes `sm`/`md`, optional leading icon. Convenience text init. **Also defines `KnotChip`** — a tappable, optionally-selected variant for multi-select pickers and filter pills. |
| `KnotInput.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | `TextField` (single-line) and `TextEditor` (multi-line) wrapper with adaptive border states (`neutral`/`focused`/`error`/`success`), optional leading icon and trailing accessory. `@FocusState` drives the focused state automatically. **Step 18.19:** Added `.contentShape(Rectangle()) + .onTapGesture { isFocused = true }` to the outer styled container so taps anywhere on the rounded card route to the inner field. Without this, SwiftUI's `TextField` only registers taps on its actual text-content area, leaving padded-edge taps to fall through to the background `Color` view — the field would silently not focus and the keyboard wouldn't open. |
| `KnotListRow.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Row primitive with leading icon, title, optional subtitle, configurable trailing accessory. Static factories: `chevron(...)` (tappable with chevron right), `info(...)` (non-tappable with right-aligned value), `toggle(...)` (with `Toggle` accessory), `action(...)` (tappable, no chevron). The generic init takes a `@ViewBuilder trailing` for custom accessories. Folds in the previously private `settingsRow`/`settingsInfoRow`/`settingsToggleRow` helpers. |
| `KnotSectionHeader.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Section header with two styles: `caption` (uppercase tertiary text, Settings-style) and `subhead` (semibold primary text with optional Lucide icon, Home/ForYou-style). Optional trailing `@ViewBuilder` for "View All"-type actions. |
| `KnotProgressIndicator.swift` | **Active (Step 18.1)** | Namespace enum with two views: `Inline` (tinted `ProgressView`) and `Overlay` (full-screen `Theme.overlayDim` + centered `ultraThinMaterial` card with optional message). The Overlay replaces the duplicated deletion / export / login loading patterns. |
| `KnotTabBar.swift` | **Active (Step 18.3, height tightened in Step 18.9, frame-height removed in Step 18.11)** | Airbnb-style custom bottom tab bar. Generic over a `Hashable` ID so callers use any tag type (e.g. `MainTabView.AppTab`). API: `selection: Binding<ID>` + `[Item]` where each `Item` carries `id`, `title`, `systemImage` (SF Symbol name; `.fill` variant applied automatically when selected via `.symbolVariant(.fill)`), and `hasNotification: Bool = false` (renders a small red dot overlaid topTrailing on the icon). Top hairline `Divider` painted with `Theme.surfaceBorder`. Active icon+label render with `Theme.accent`; inactive with `Theme.textTertiary`. Animates color/icon transitions with `Theme.Motion.quick`. Provides `.sensoryFeedback(.selection, ...)` haptic on tab change (iOS 17+). Mounted by callers via `.safeAreaInset(edge: .bottom)` so destination views' insets shrink correctly. Replaces the previous SwiftUI `TabView` + `UITabBarAppearance` setup in `MainTabView`. **Step 18.9:** introduced `HStack(alignment: .center)`, `.padding(.top, Theme.Spacing.lg)` (16pt) above the icons, and removed all `.ignoresSafeArea` from the bar — the home-indicator safe area below now shows the parent's background instead of an empty strip of bar-colored space. **Step 18.11:** removed the 32pt `.frame(height:)` constraint Step 18.9 had also added — the VStack now sizes to its intrinsic content (~61pt: divider + top padding + icon + spacing + label + button padding). The previous fixed frame was smaller than the bar's painted content, which caused `.safeAreaInset(edge: .bottom)` in `MainTabView` to under-reserve space and let tab content (notably the Version row in the Profile/About section) hide behind the bar. With the frame gone, the inset reservation tracks the bar's actual rendered height automatically. |

#### `/Resources` — Assets
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `Assets.xcassets/` | App icon, accent color, and image assets |
| `Assets.xcassets/Interests/` | **Namespaced folder group** (`provides-namespace: true`) containing 40 image sets, convention `interest-{lowercased-hyphenated}` (e.g., `interest-travel`, `interest-board-games`). Each set holds a JPEG (~280x400px). Previously used as interest **card** backgrounds via `OnboardingInterestsView.imageName(for:)`. **Step 18.30 (2026-06-07):** the interests/dislikes screens became flat icon-row lists, so `imageName(for:)` was deleted and these image sets are **no longer referenced** by app code (kept in the catalog for now; safe to prune in a later cleanup). |
| `Colors.xcassets/` | Named colors for the design system |
| `Fonts/` | **Step 18.10, bundled in Step 18.12.** Custom font `.ttf` files for the Fraunces + DM Sans typography pairing. Bundles `Fraunces-VariableFont_SOFT,WONK,opsz,wght.ttf` (family `Fraunces` — a single variable font covering Light through Black via the `wght` axis) plus four DM Sans static cuts (`DMSans-Regular.ttf`, `DMSans-Medium.ttf`, `DMSans-SemiBold.ttf`, `DMSans-Bold.ttf`). Each filename appears in `Info.plist` under `UIAppFonts`. XcodeGen's `sources: [path: Knot]` rule auto-includes anything under `iOS/Knot/`, so dropping a font file here and running `xcodegen generate` wires it into the Knot target's Copy Bundle Resources phase. `Theme.Typography` references Fraunces by family name and selects weight via `.weight(...)` against the variable font's `wght` axis; DM Sans is referenced by PostScript name (which matches each cut's filename). The italic Fraunces variable font is not bundled, so `Theme.Typography.italicQuote` uses synthesized italic (`.italic()` on the upright VF) — to upgrade to the true italic cut, bundle `Fraunces-Italic-VariableFont_*.ttf` and swap the `italicQuote` definition. Verify any change via the `Theme.registerFonts()` debug print on app launch. Both families ship under SIL OFL 1.1. |

### Test Targets

| Folder | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `KnotTests/` | Unit tests for business logic, services, and utilities. Contains `KnotTests.swift` (constants validation), `RecommendationCardTests.swift` (Step 6.1 — 12 tests: rendering with full/minimal/all-type/unknown-type data, price formatting for whole dollar/cents/GBP/zero/large amounts, select callback, long text truncation), `RecommendationsViewTests.swift` (Steps 6.2–6.4 — 35 tests total: 12 DTO tests for generate/refresh/feedback encoding+decoding, 11 ViewModel tests for initial state + currentPage + selection state management + refresh reason state management (sheet visibility, guards during refresh/animation, cardsVisible toggle), 12 view rendering tests for RecommendationsView + SelectionConfirmationSheet (confirm/cancel callbacks, all types, location data) + RefreshReasonSheet (rendering, reason callback, all 5 reasons, dark scheme)), and `SettingsViewTests.swift` (Steps 11.1–11.4 — 33 tests total: `SettingsViewModelTests` — 30 tests covering initial state, account deletion state, data export state, and notification preferences state (Step 11.4: quietHoursStart/End, isLoadingPreferences, isSavingPreferences, preferencesError, formatHour, showQuietHoursPicker); `SettingsViewRenderingTests` — 3 rendering tests (SettingsView light/dark mode, ReauthenticationSheet rendering)), and `RelationshipLengthModalTests.swift` (Step 18.29, +1 in Step 18.33 — 17 tests: `relationshipTenureSummary` singular/plural/zero formatting, `RelationshipLengthBounds` values + clamp math (no month wrap, year cap 50, lower-bound clamp), decompose/recompose round-trip, light/dark render smoke tests for `RelationshipLengthField` + `RelationshipLengthModal`, and a required-placeholder-state render test). All test classes are `@MainActor` for Swift 6 concurrency compliance. |
| `KnotUITests/` | UI tests for critical user flows (onboarding, hint capture) |

---

## Backend (`backend/`)

```
backend/
├── app/
│   ├── __init__.py           # App package marker
│   ├── main.py               # FastAPI entry point, app factory, /health endpoint, router registration
│   ├── api/                  # Route handlers (one file per API domain)
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── deeplinks.py      # AASA endpoint + web fallback (Step 9.1) — no /api/v1 prefix
│   │   ├── vault.py          # POST/PUT/GET /api/v1/vault — Partner Vault CRUD
│   │   ├── hints.py          # POST/GET/DELETE /api/v1/hints — Hint capture & retrieval
│   │   ├── recommendations.py # POST /api/v1/recommendations — Generation, refresh, feedback, GET by-milestone (Step 7.7), GET by-id (Step 9.2)
│   │   ├── milestones.py     # GET/POST/PUT/DELETE /api/v1/milestones — Post-onboarding milestone CRUD (Step 17.1)
│   │   ├── notifications.py  # POST /api/v1/notifications/process + GET /history + PATCH /viewed (Step 7.7)
│   │   └── users.py          # POST /api/v1/users/device-token + DELETE /api/v1/users/me — Device token registration and account deletion
│   ├── core/                 # Configuration & cross-cutting concerns
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── config.py         # App settings (API prefix, project name, env vars)
│   │   └── security.py       # Auth middleware — validates Supabase JWT Bearer tokens
│   ├── models/               # Pydantic schemas for request/response validation
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── vault.py          # Vault request/response models with validation constants
│   │   ├── hints.py          # Hint request/response models (Step 4.2) — HintCreateRequest (500-char validation), HintCreateResponse, HintListResponse, HintResponse
│   │   ├── recommendations.py # Recommendation models (Steps 5.9–6.3, updated 17.1) — GenerateRequest, RefreshRequest, RecommendationFeedbackRequest (action Literal + rating validator), RecommendationFeedbackResponse, response models with briefing_text/briefing_snippet and "plan" type
│   │   ├── milestones.py     # Milestone CRUD models (Step 17.1) — MilestoneCreateRequest, MilestoneUpdateRequest, MilestoneItemResponse, MilestoneListResponse
│   │   └── users.py          # User models (Step 7.4) — DeviceTokenRequest (stripped, non-empty, max 200, platform validation), DeviceTokenResponse
│   ├── services/             # Business logic layer
│   │   ├── __init__.py

│       ├── 00015_add_viewed_at_to_notification_queue.sql # Adds viewed_at TIMESTAMPTZ nullable to notification_queue for tracking when user views recommendations (Step 7.7)

│   ├── test_account_deletion_api.py # Step 11.2: Verifies DELETE /api/v1/users/me account deletion — TestValidDeletion (200 with status "deleted", auth user removed from auth.users, public user row removed via CASCADE) (3 tests), TestAuthRequired (no auth header 401, invalid token 401) (2 tests), TestModuleImports (AccountDeleteResponse importable, defaults correct, DELETE route registered, existing device-token route still registered) (4 tests) (9 tests: 9 pass + 0 skip)
│   ├── test_dev_reset_api.py        # Step 15.6: Verifies POST /api/v1/users/me/dev-reset DEBUG-only reset — TestProductionGate (403 when DEV_RESET_ENABLED=false) (1 test), TestHappyPath (200 reset status, partner_vaults deleted, CASCADE children removed, scheduled_deletion_at cleared, idempotent on no-vault) (5 tests), TestAuthRequired (no auth 401, invalid token 401) (2 tests), TestPendingDeletionUserCanReset (works for grace-window users — uses get_current_user_id) (1 test), TestModuleImports (config flag imports, route registered, sibling /me routes intact) (3 tests) (12 tests: 12 pass + 0 skip)
│   ├── test_data_export_api.py    # Step 11.3: Verifies GET /api/v1/users/me/export data export — TestExportWithVault (200 with exported_at timestamp, user section with id/email/created_at, vault with partner_name/interests/dislikes/vibes/budgets/love_languages, milestones list, hints list with correct fields excluding embeddings, recommendations list, feedback list, notifications list) (13 tests), TestExportWithoutVault (200 with user data, null vault, empty collections) (4 tests), TestAuthRequired (no auth header 401, invalid token 401) (2 tests), TestModuleImports (DataExportResponse importable, defaults correct, GET /me/export route registered, existing device-token and DELETE /me routes still registered) (5 tests) (24 tests: 24 pass + 0 skip)
│   ├── test_notification_preferences_api.py # Step 11.4: Verifies GET/PUT /api/v1/users/me/notification-preferences and webhook integration — TestGetDefaultPreferences (200, defaults true/22/8/null) (4 tests), TestUpdatePreferences (quiet hours, notifications_enabled, timezone, partial update, reflects on GET, single field) (6 tests), TestValidation (negative hours rejected, >23 rejected, invalid timezone, valid timezone, edge case hour 0) (5 tests), TestAuthRequired (GET/PUT no auth 401, GET/PUT invalid token 401) (4 tests), TestModuleImports (models importable, defaults correct, GET/PUT routes registered, existing routes preserved) (7 tests), TestWebhookNotificationsDisabled (disabled skips, enabled processes) (2 tests) (28 tests: 28 pass + 0 skip)
│   ├── test_briefing_generation.py # Step 17.1: Verifies briefing generation service — prompt construction (milestone context, partner profile, hints with IDs), Claude generation with mocked API, hint ID filtering/validation, snippet truncation to 100 chars, error handling (10 tests)
│   └── test_milestone_crud.py     # Step 17.1: Verifies milestone CRUD — model validation (create/update requests, item response), next occurrence date computation, plan type validation in state/generation, APNs briefing snippet behavior (17 tests)
├── venv/                     # Python 3.13 virtual environment (gitignored)
├── requirements.txt          # Python dependencies (all packages for MVP)
├── pyproject.toml            # Pytest configuration (asyncio mode, warning filters)
├── .env.example              # Template for environment variables (safe to commit)
├── .env                      # Actual secrets (gitignored, NEVER commit)
└── .gitignore                # Excludes .env, __pycache__, venv, IDE files
```

### Entry Point (`app/main.py`)

| Symbol | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `app` | The FastAPI application instance. Title: "Knot API", version: "0.1.0". |
| `vault_router` | Imported from `app.api.vault` and registered via `app.include_router(vault_router)`. Provides `POST /api/v1/vault`, `GET /api/v1/vault`, `PUT /api/v1/vault`. |
| `hints_router` | **Added in Step 4.2, updated Step 4.6.** Imported from `app.api.hints` and registered via `app.include_router(hints_router)`. Provides `POST /api/v1/hints`, `GET /api/v1/hints`, `DELETE /api/v1/hints/{hint_id}`. |
| `recommendations_router` | **Added in Step 5.9, updated Step 5.10.** Imported from `app.api.recommendations` and registered via `app.include_router(recommendations_router)`. Provides `POST /api/v1/recommendations/generate`, `POST /api/v1/recommendations/refresh`. |
| `users_router` | **Added in Step 7.4, updated Step 11.2, extended Step 15.5 and Step 15.6.** Imported from `app.api.users` and registered via `app.include_router(users_router)`. Provides `POST /device-token`, `GET /me`, `DELETE /me`, `POST /me/restore`, `POST /me/dev-reset` (DEBUG-only, gated by `KNOT_DEV_RESET_ENABLED`), `POST /process-deletion` (QStash webhook), `GET /me/export`, `GET`/`PUT /me/notification-preferences`. |
| `health_check()` | `GET /health` — Returns `{"status": "ok"}`. Unprotected. Used by deployment platforms for uptime monitoring. |
| `get_current_user()` | `GET /api/v1/me` — **Protected** endpoint that returns `{"user_id": "<uuid>"}`. Uses `Depends(get_current_user_id)` to validate the Bearer token. Serves as a "who am I" endpoint and auth middleware verification route. Added in Step 2.5. |

API routers from `app/api/` are registered here via `app.include_router()`. Currently registered: `deeplinks_router`, `feedback_router`, `vault_router`, `hints_router`, `ideas_router`, `milestones_router`, `recommendations_router`, `notifications_router`, `users_router`.

### Route Handlers (`app/api/`)

Each file defines an `APIRouter` with a URL prefix and tag.

| File | Prefix | Status | Responsibility |
|------|--------|--------|----------------|
| `vault.py` | `/api/v1/vault` | **Active (Step 3.12)** | Three endpoints: (1) `POST` — Accepts full onboarding payload, validates with Pydantic, inserts into 6 tables. Returns 201/409/422. (2) `GET` — Loads user's vault from all 6 tables, separates interests into likes/dislikes, returns milestones/budgets with DB `id`s, love languages with priority. Returns 200/404. (3) `PUT` — Accepts same payload as POST, uses "replace all" strategy (update vault row, delete + re-insert all child rows), preserves vault_id. Returns 200/404/422. All endpoints use `get_service_client()` (bypasses RLS) with user identity validated by auth middleware. Private helper `_cleanup_vault()` handles partial failure cleanup for POST. |
| `hints.py` | `/api/v1/hints` | **Active (Step 4.6)** | Three endpoints: (1) `POST` — Validates hint text (non-empty, ≤500 chars via Pydantic `@field_validator`), looks up user's vault_id from `partner_vaults`, generates 768-dim embedding via `generate_embedding()` from `app.services.embedding` (Vertex AI `text-embedding-004`, async via `asyncio.to_thread()`), formats via `format_embedding_for_pgvector()`, inserts into `hints` table. If embedding generation fails or Vertex AI is unconfigured, hint is still saved with `hint_embedding = NULL` (graceful degradation). Logs embedding status via `logging.getLogger`. Returns 201/404/422/500. (2) `GET` — Lists hints in reverse chronological order (`ORDER BY created_at DESC`), selects display columns only (excludes `hint_embedding`), supports `limit`/`offset` pagination via Query params, returns total count via `count="exact"`. Returns 200/404. (3) `DELETE /{hint_id}` — Validates the hint exists and belongs to the authenticated user's vault (vault_id ownership check), then hard-deletes the hint from the database. Returns 404 (not 403) for unauthorized access to prevent information leakage. Returns 204/404/500. All endpoints use `get_service_client()` with auth via `get_current_user_id`. |
| `recommendations.py` | `/api/v1/recommendations` | **Active (Step 9.2)** | Four endpoints: (1) `POST /generate` — Accepts `RecommendationGenerateRequest` (occasion_type + optional milestone_id), loads the user's vault from all 6 tables (interests split into likes/dislikes, vibes, budgets mapped to `VaultBudget`, love languages parsed into primary/secondary), determines budget range via `_find_budget_range()` (matches occasion_type or falls back to defaults: just_because $20–50, minor_occasion $50–150, major_milestone $100–500), optionally loads milestone context (validates vault ownership), builds `RecommendationState`, runs `run_recommendation_pipeline()` from Step 5.8, stores 3 results in `recommendations` table (non-fatal on failure), returns `RecommendationGenerateResponse` with DB-generated UUIDs, scoring metadata, and optional location data. Returns 200/401/404/422/500. (2) `POST /refresh` — Accepts `RecommendationRefreshRequest` (rejected_recommendation_ids + rejection_reason enum), loads rejected recommendations from DB, stores feedback with `action='refreshed'` in `recommendation_feedback` table, re-runs the full pipeline, applies exclusion filters based on rejection reason (`too_expensive`: exclude candidates at/above rejected price tier; `too_cheap`: exclude at/below; `not_their_style`: exclude matching vibe metadata; `already_have_similar`: exclude same merchant+type combos; `show_different`: exclude by title match only), stores new results, returns `RecommendationRefreshResponse`. Returns 200/401/404/422/500. **Shared helpers:** `_fallback_image_url(candidate)` (Step 16.2) — returns a curated Unsplash URL based on candidate's `matched_interests` or `matched_vibes` by importing `_INTEREST_IMAGES`/`_VIBE_IMAGES` from `aggregation.py`; used as fallback when `candidate.image_url` is None. `_build_response_items(candidates, db_result)` builds response items with DB-generated UUIDs (used by both generate and refresh endpoints), applies `_fallback_image_url()` when `candidate.image_url` is None so all responses have images. `_classify_price_tier(price_cents, budget_range)` splits budget into low/mid/high thirds, `_apply_exclusion_filters(candidates, rejected_recs, rejection_reason, budget_range)` applies reason-specific filtering with title-based exclusion as the baseline for all reasons. Uses `get_service_client()` with auth via `get_current_user_id`. **Step 7.7:** `GET /by-milestone/{milestone_id}` — authenticated via `Depends(get_current_user_id)`, looks up user's vault_id, queries `recommendations` WHERE vault_id AND milestone_id, returns up to 10 pre-generated recommendations (read-only, no pipeline execution). Returns `MilestoneRecommendationsResponse`. Returns 200/401/404. **Step 9.2:** `GET /{recommendation_id}` — authenticated via `Depends(get_current_user_id)`, looks up user's vault_id, queries `recommendations` by ID, verifies vault_id match (returns 404 for both not-found and wrong-owner to prevent ID enumeration). Returns `MilestoneRecommendationItem`. **CRITICAL:** This route MUST be the LAST registered route on the router because `/{recommendation_id}` is a catch-all path parameter that would shadow `/generate`, `/refresh`, `/feedback`, and `/by-milestone/{id}` if placed before them. Returns 200/401/404/500. |
| `notifications.py` | `/api/v1/notifications` | **Active (Step 11.4)** | QStash webhook endpoint for processing scheduled notifications plus user-facing history endpoints. Three endpoints: `POST /process` — receives webhook calls from Upstash QStash, reads raw request body for signature verification, validates `Upstash-Signature` JWT header via `verify_qstash_signature()` (returns 401 on failure), parses `NotificationProcessRequest` payload (notification_id, user_id, milestone_id, days_before), looks up the `notification_queue` entry via service client, skips already-processed notifications (returns `status: "skipped"` for sent/failed/cancelled). Step 7.3: generates recommendations via `run_recommendation_pipeline()` and stores in DB. Step 7.6: calls `check_quiet_hours(user_id)` — returns 3-tuple `(is_quiet, next_delivery, notifications_enabled)`. **Step 11.4:** If `notifications_enabled` is `False`, skips processing and returns `status: "skipped"`, `message: "Notifications disabled by user."` (checked before quiet hours). If quiet, republishes to QStash with `not_before` = next delivery time and returns `status: "rescheduled"`. Step 7.5: delivers APNs push via `deliver_push_notification()`. Updates pending notifications to `status: "sent"` with `sent_at` timestamp. Does NOT use `get_current_user_id` auth dependency — authentication is via QStash signature, not user Bearer tokens. Returns `NotificationProcessResponse` (status, notification_id, message, recommendations_generated, push_delivered). Returns 200/401/404/422/500. **Step 7.7:** `GET /history` — authenticated via `Depends(get_current_user_id)`, queries `notification_queue` WHERE user_id AND status IN ('sent', 'failed'), joins milestone metadata from `partner_milestones` (graceful "Deleted Milestone" fallback), counts recommendations per milestone from `recommendations` table, supports `limit`/`offset` pagination (defaults 50/0), returns `NotificationHistoryResponse`. `PATCH /{notification_id}/viewed` — authenticated, validates user ownership via user_id filter, sets `viewed_at` timestamp, returns 200/404. |
| `users.py` | `/api/v1/users` | **Active (Step 15.6)** | Endpoints: (1) `POST /device-token` — registers/updates the APNs token. Uses `get_active_user_id`. (2) `GET /me` (Step 15.5) — lightweight account-status probe returning `{user_id, scheduled_deletion_at}`. Uses `get_current_user_id` so pending users can read the scheduled date. (3) `DELETE /me` (Step 15.5) — **soft delete**. Sets `scheduled_deletion_at = now() + 60 days` on `public.users` and publishes a QStash purge job with `not_before=<unix-ts>` to `POST /api/v1/users/process-deletion`. Returns `AccountDeleteResponse(scheduled_deletion_at=...)`. Uses `get_current_user_id` (so a re-tap re-schedules instead of 410-ing). (4) `POST /me/restore` (Step 15.5) — clears `scheduled_deletion_at`. Idempotent. Uses `get_current_user_id` (pending users must be able to call this). (5) `POST /me/dev-reset` (Step 15.6, **DEBUG-only**) — gated by `DEV_RESET_ENABLED` (returns 403 unless `KNOT_DEV_RESET_ENABLED=true`). Clears `scheduled_deletion_at` and deletes the caller's `partner_vaults` row; CASCADE removes all child rows. The `users` row is preserved (device token, quiet hours stay). Uses `get_current_user_id` so users mid-grace-window can also reset. Returns `{"status": "reset", "user_id": "..."}`. (6) `POST /process-deletion` (Step 15.5) — QStash webhook. Verifies the Upstash-Signature JWT, re-reads `scheduled_deletion_at`, then hard-deletes via the Supabase Admin API (`DELETE {SUPABASE_URL}/auth/v1/admin/users/{user_id}`) only if the column is still set and in the past. Maps a 404 from the admin API to success for idempotent replays. (7) `GET /me/export` — unchanged JSON export, now via `get_active_user_id`. (8,9) `GET`/`PUT /me/notification-preferences` — unchanged, now via `get_active_user_id`. Helper `_hard_delete_auth_user(user_id)` factored out the admin-API call for reuse by the worker. |
| `milestones.py` | `/api/v1/milestones` | **Active (Step 17.1)** | Post-onboarding milestone CRUD. Four endpoints: (1) `GET` — Lists all milestones for the user's vault with computed `days_until` via `_compute_days_until()` (uses `compute_next_occurrence()` from notification_scheduler). (2) `POST` — Creates a single milestone, inserts into `partner_milestones`, schedules notifications via `schedule_milestone_notifications()`. Returns 201. (3) `PUT /{id}` — Updates milestone fields, deletes pending `notification_queue` entries and reschedules if date/recurrence changed. (4) `DELETE /{id}` — Deletes milestone (CASCADE removes notifications). Helper: `_get_vault_id()` looks up user's vault, `_build_milestone_response()` constructs response items. All endpoints use `get_current_user_id` auth. |
| `deeplinks.py` | *(no prefix)* | **Active (Step 9.1)** | Three public endpoints, all unauthenticated: (1) `GET /.well-known/apple-app-site-association` — serves the AASA JSON with `Content-Type: application/json`. Contains `applinks.details[0].appIDs = ["VN5G3R8J23.com.ronniejay.knot"]` and `components = [{ "/": "/recommendation/*" }]` using the modern iOS 15+ components format. Also includes `webcredentials.apps` for future web auth support. (2) `GET /apple-app-site-association` — identical AASA content at the legacy root path (Apple checks both locations). (3) `GET /recommendation/{recommendation_id}` — HTML web fallback page for users without the app installed. Renders a dark-gradient branded page matching the app aesthetic with "Coming Soon on the App Store" placeholder and a truncated recommendation ID reference. The router has NO prefix (unlike all other routers) because Apple requires the AASA at the domain root. Registered first in `main.py` for route priority. |

### Configuration (`app/core/`)

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `config.py` | Loads environment variables from `.env` via `python-dotenv`. Exposes `SUPABASE_URL`, `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, `GOOGLE_CLOUD_PROJECT`, `GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS`, and future API keys. **QStash vars (Step 7.1):** `UPSTASH_QSTASH_TOKEN`, `UPSTASH_QSTASH_URL` (defaults to `https://qstash.upstash.io`), `QSTASH_CURRENT_SIGNING_KEY`, `QSTASH_NEXT_SIGNING_KEY`. **APNs vars (Step 7.5):** `APNS_KEY_ID`, `APNS_TEAM_ID`, `APNS_AUTH_KEY_PATH` (filesystem path to .p8 key), `APNS_BUNDLE_ID` (app bundle identifier for apns-topic header), `APNS_USE_SANDBOX` (bool, defaults to `true`). **Shopify vars (Step 8.4):** `SHOPIFY_STOREFRONT_TOKEN`, `SHOPIFY_STORE_DOMAIN`. **Universal Links (Step 9.1):** `APP_DOMAIN` (defaults to `api.knot-app.com`). Provides `validate_supabase_config()` to check required Supabase vars, `validate_vertex_ai_config()` / `is_vertex_ai_configured()` for Vertex AI, `validate_qstash_config()` / `is_qstash_configured()` for QStash, `validate_apns_config()` / `is_apns_configured()` for APNs, and `validate_shopify_config()` / `is_shopify_configured()` for Shopify (all non-fatal, return `bool`). |
| `security.py` | **Auth middleware (Step 2.5).** Exports `get_current_user_id` — a FastAPI dependency that extracts the Bearer token from the `Authorization` header via `HTTPBearer(auto_error=False)`, validates it against Supabase Auth's `/auth/v1/user` endpoint using `httpx.AsyncClient`, and returns the authenticated user's UUID string. Raises `HTTPException(401)` with `WWW-Authenticate: Bearer` header for all failure cases: missing token, invalid/expired token, network errors, and malformed responses. Uses a private `_get_apikey()` helper with lazy import of `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` to avoid circular dependencies. Usage: `async def route(user_id: str = Depends(get_current_user_id))`. |

### Data Layer (`app/models/`, `app/db/`)

| Folder/File | Purpose |
|-------------|---------|
| `models/` | Pydantic models for API request/response validation. Ensures strict schema adherence (e.g., at least 5 interests, valid vibe tags, ≤500 char hints). |
| `models/vault.py` | **Active (Step 3.12; Step 18.24 — 2026-05-31).** Vault request/response schemas. **Constants:** `VALID_INTEREST_CATEGORIES` (40 seed values, no longer authoritative), `VALID_VIBE_TAGS` (8), `VALID_LOVE_LANGUAGES` (5) — `set[str]`. `MAX_INTEREST_NAME_LENGTH = 50` caps custom interest/dislike names. **Shared helper:** `_validate_interest_list(v, *, label)` trims each entry, rejects empty/whitespace, enforces the 50-char cap, de-duplicates case-insensitively, and enforces the at-least-5 minimum — used by both `validate_interests` and `validate_dislikes`. **Request sub-models:** `MilestoneCreate` (`@model_validator` requiring budget_tier for custom), `BudgetCreate` (`@model_validator` enforcing max >= min >= 0), `LoveLanguagesCreate` (`@model_validator` enforcing different primary/secondary). **Main request:** `VaultCreateRequest` — used for both POST and PUT — field validators for counts (5/5/3, ≥1), free-form interest/dislike names (no allowlist as of Step 18.24), uniqueness, birthday requirement, cross-field `@model_validator` preventing case-insensitive interest/dislike overlap. **POST response:** `VaultCreateResponse` (vault_id, summary counts). **GET response (Step 3.12):** `VaultGetResponse` (full vault data from all 6 tables), `MilestoneResponse` (id, type, name, date, recurrence, budget_tier), `BudgetResponse` (id, occasion_type, min/max, currency), `LoveLanguageResponse` (language, priority). **PUT response (Step 3.12):** `VaultUpdateResponse` (mirrors VaultCreateResponse). |
| `models/hints.py` | **Active (Step 4.2).** Hint request/response schemas. **Constants:** `MAX_HINT_LENGTH = 500`. **Request:** `HintCreateRequest` — `hint_text` (str, `@field_validator` strips whitespace, rejects empty, enforces ≤500 chars), `source` (str, default `"text_input"`). **Responses:** `HintResponse` (id, hint_text, source, is_used, created_at), `HintCreateResponse` (same fields — returned on successful creation), `HintListResponse` (hints: list[HintResponse], total: int — for paginated list endpoint). |
| `models/recommendations.py` | **Active (Step 5.10).** Recommendation request/response schemas. **Generate request:** `RecommendationGenerateRequest` — `milestone_id` (optional str), `occasion_type` (Literal `just_because\|minor_occasion\|major_milestone`). **Refresh request:** `RecommendationRefreshRequest` — `rejected_recommendation_ids` (list[str], `@field_validator` enforces non-empty), `rejection_reason` (Literal `too_expensive\|too_cheap\|not_their_style\|already_have_similar\|show_different`). **Shared responses:** `LocationResponse` (optional city/state/country/address for experience/date recs), `RecommendationItemResponse` (id, recommendation_type Literal `gift\|experience\|date`, title, optional description/price_cents/image_url/merchant_name, currency default "USD", external_url, source, optional LocationResponse, 4 scoring floats: interest_score/vibe_score/love_language_score/final_score all default 0.0). **Generate response:** `RecommendationGenerateResponse` (recommendations: list[RecommendationItemResponse], count: int, optional milestone_id, occasion_type). **Refresh response:** `RecommendationRefreshResponse` (recommendations: list[RecommendationItemResponse], count: int, rejection_reason: str). |
| `models/notifications.py` | **Active (Step 7.1, updated 7.3, 7.5, 7.7).** Notification webhook request/response schemas plus notification history models. **Request:** `NotificationProcessRequest` — `notification_id` (str, UUID of notification_queue entry), `user_id` (str), `milestone_id` (str), `days_before` (int, 14/7/3). **Response:** `NotificationProcessResponse` — `status` (str: 'processed'/'skipped'/'failed'), `notification_id` (str), `message` (str, human-readable description), `recommendations_generated` (int, default 0 — Step 7.3), `push_delivered` (bool, default False — Step 7.5, True when APNs push was successfully accepted). **Step 7.7 history models:** `NotificationHistoryItem` (id, milestone_id, milestone_name, milestone_type, milestone_date, days_before, status, sent_at nullable, viewed_at nullable, created_at, recommendations_count default 0), `NotificationHistoryResponse` (notifications: list[NotificationHistoryItem], total: int default 0), `MilestoneRecommendationItem` (id, recommendation_type, title, description nullable, external_url nullable, price_cents nullable, merchant_name nullable, image_url nullable, created_at), `MilestoneRecommendationsResponse` (recommendations: list[MilestoneRecommendationItem], count: int default 0, milestone_id). |
| `models/users.py` | **Active (Step 15.5).** User account request/response schemas. **Device token:** `DeviceTokenRequest`/`DeviceTokenResponse` (unchanged). **Soft-delete (Step 15.5):** `AccountDeleteResponse` — `status` default `"scheduled"`, `scheduled_deletion_at` (str, required ISO 8601), `message`. `AccountRestoreResponse` — `status` default `"restored"`, `message`. `AccountStatusResponse` — `user_id` (str), `scheduled_deletion_at` (str nullable). **Notification preferences (Step 11.4):** `NotificationPreferencesResponse`/`NotificationPreferencesRequest` (unchanged). **Data export:** `DataExportResponse` (unchanged). |
| `core/security.py` | **Active (Step 15.5).** Two FastAPI dependencies. `get_current_user_id` validates the Supabase JWT and returns the user UUID — 401s on missing/invalid/expired token. `get_active_user_id` wraps `get_current_user_id` and additionally reads `public.users.scheduled_deletion_at`; when non-null it raises HTTP 410 Gone with body `{"detail": {"code": "account_pending_deletion", "scheduled_deletion_at": "<iso>"}}`. Every authenticated route in `app/api/` uses `get_active_user_id` **except** `DELETE /users/me` (so a re-tap re-schedules rather than 410-ing), `POST /users/me/restore` (so pending users can recover), and `GET /users/me` (so the iOS client can read the scheduled date). |
| `db/` | Database connection and repository pattern classes. |
| `db/supabase_client.py` | Provides two lazy-initialized Supabase clients: `get_supabase_client()` uses the anon key (respects RLS for user-scoped queries) and `get_service_client()` uses the service_role key (bypasses RLS for admin/background operations). Also provides `test_connection()` to verify database connectivity. |

### Supabase Migrations (`supabase/migrations/`)

SQL migration files to be run in the Supabase SQL Editor or via `supabase db push`.

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `00001_enable_pgvector.sql` | Enables the `vector` extension (pgvector) required for hint embedding storage and similarity search. Must be run before creating any tables with `vector(768)` columns. |
| `00002_create_users_table.sql` | Creates `public.users` table (id, email, created_at, updated_at) linked to `auth.users` via FK with CASCADE delete. Enables RLS with SELECT/UPDATE/INSERT policies enforcing `auth.uid() = id`. Creates two trigger functions: `handle_updated_at()` (reusable, auto-updates timestamp on row changes) and `handle_new_user()` (SECURITY DEFINER, auto-creates profile on auth signup). Grants permissions to `authenticated` and `anon` roles. |
| `00003_create_partner_vaults_table.sql` | Creates `public.partner_vaults` table (id, user_id, partner_name, relationship_tenure_months, cohabitation_status, location_city, location_state, location_country, created_at, updated_at). `user_id` is UNIQUE (one vault per user) with FK CASCADE to `public.users`. CHECK constraint on `cohabitation_status` for 3 valid enum values. `location_country` defaults to `'US'`. Reuses `handle_updated_at()` trigger from migration 00002. RLS policies enforce `auth.uid() = user_id` for all 4 operations (SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE). |
| `00004_create_partner_interests_table.sql` | Creates `public.partner_interests` table (id, vault_id, interest_type, interest_category, created_at). Original CHECK on `interest_category` listed 40 predefined categories; **dropped in migration 00025 (Step 18.24)** so users can add custom interests/dislikes during onboarding. CHECK on `interest_type` ('like'/'dislike') remains. `UNIQUE(vault_id, interest_category)` still prevents duplicate categories and blocks the same interest as both like and dislike. FK CASCADE to `partner_vaults`. RLS policies use subquery to `partner_vaults` to check ownership via `auth.uid() = user_id`. Index on `vault_id` for fast lookups. "At least 5 likes + 5 dislikes (no upper bound)" + length / non-emptiness enforced at the API layer (`backend/app/models/vault.py`). |
| `00025_allow_custom_interest_categories.sql` | **Active (Step 18.24 — 2026-05-31).** Drops the `interest_category` CHECK constraint on `partner_interests` so the iOS onboarding flow can add custom interests/dislikes from the search bar. Keeps `UNIQUE(vault_id, interest_category)`. Updates the column comment to reflect the new free-form behavior; Pydantic now owns length + emptiness checks (50-char cap, case-insensitive dedup). |
| `00005_create_partner_milestones_table.sql` | Creates `public.partner_milestones` table (id, vault_id, milestone_type, milestone_name, milestone_date, recurrence, budget_tier, created_at). Three CHECK constraints: `milestone_type` for 4 types (birthday/anniversary/holiday/custom), `recurrence` for yearly/one_time, `budget_tier` for 3 tiers. Creates `handle_milestone_budget_tier()` BEFORE INSERT trigger that auto-sets budget_tier when not provided: birthday/anniversary → major_milestone, holiday → minor_occasion, custom → must be explicit (NULL rejected by NOT NULL). No UNIQUE constraint on (vault_id, milestone_type) — multiple milestones of same type allowed (e.g., multiple holidays). FK CASCADE to `partner_vaults`. RLS uses subquery pattern. Index on `vault_id`. |
| `00006_create_partner_vibes_table.sql` | Creates `public.partner_vibes` table (id, vault_id, vibe_tag, created_at). CHECK constraint on `vibe_tag` for 8 valid aesthetic values: quiet_luxury, street_urban, outdoorsy, vintage, minimalist, bohemian, romantic, adventurous. `UNIQUE(vault_id, vibe_tag)` prevents duplicate vibes per vault (same deduplication pattern as `partner_interests`). No trigger functions needed — vibes are simple tag storage with no computed defaults. "Minimum 1, maximum 4 vibes per vault" enforced at API layer, not database. FK CASCADE to `partner_vaults`. RLS uses subquery pattern. Index on `vault_id`. |
| `00007_create_partner_budgets_table.sql` | Creates `public.partner_budgets` table (id, vault_id, occasion_type, min_amount, max_amount, currency, created_at). CHECK constraint on `occasion_type` for 3 budget tiers: just_because, minor_occasion, major_milestone. Two cross-column CHECK constraints: `max_amount >= min_amount` (prevents invalid ranges) and `min_amount >= 0` (prevents negative amounts). Amounts stored as **integers in cents** (e.g., 2000 = $20.00) to avoid floating-point precision issues. `UNIQUE(vault_id, occasion_type)` ensures one budget per occasion type per vault. `currency` defaults to `'USD'` — international users can override. No trigger functions needed — budgets are direct value storage. "Exactly 3 tiers per vault" enforced at API layer, not database. FK CASCADE to `partner_vaults`. RLS uses subquery pattern. Index on `vault_id`. |
| `00008_create_partner_love_languages_table.sql` | Creates `public.partner_love_languages` table (id, vault_id, language, priority, created_at). CHECK constraint on `language` for 5 valid values: words_of_affirmation, acts_of_service, receiving_gifts, quality_time, physical_touch.
